Foreign Newspapers Resist

(Berlin) Propaganda Minister Goebbels recently delivered a speech condemning foreign reporters for transmitting many false reports about the recent purge in Germany. Now, the Berlin Foreign Press Association has risen to resist. Today, the association passed a resolution by a vote of 55 to 5 announcing that Goebbels's accusations have been answered by world public opinion, and stated that foreign reporters in Germany have always valued fairness and accuracy, and that the first condition for their inquiries is to be accurate, reliable, and quick. (Reuters dispatch from the 13th)

Johnson Criticizes Hitler - United States Apologizes to Germany

(Washington) General Johnson, the director of the American Recovery Administration, attacked German Chancellor Hitler's indiscriminate killing of political opponents in a speech in Waterloo, which almost became an international problem between the United States and Germany. However, the State Department quickly took steps to avoid it. After the German chargé d'affaires in the United States, Leitner, formally protested, the State Department immediately expressed its apology, but said that General Johnson was expressing his personal opinion and not speaking on behalf of the US government. Observers believe that this matter has come to an end, which can be called one of the fastest resolved matters in diplomatic history. General Johnson heard of the German protest in Omaha and replied, "I am responsible for what I said and will never withdraw it. The State Department may not order me to withdraw it either." He only stated that his remarks were his personal opinion and did not represent the government. He believed that the brutality of the National Socialist Party showed how far a country's constitution could fall after being overthrown. (National dispatch from the 13th)

General Johnson, director of the National Recovery Administration in Omaha, went to the Pacific coast. He passed through here today and said that he expected the US State Department to condemn him for his remarks denouncing the German purge, but he would not change his position because of this, because the brutal actions of Germany really made him feel distressed. Soviet Russia Mechanized - National Wartime Preparation

(Moscow) Soviet Russian factories are actively carrying out mechanization under wartime conditions, in order to free up manpower for emergencies. Therefore, once war breaks out, tens of thousands of Soviet Russian workers can join the army together, and the factories will not be closed. The Soviet Russian authorities declared that they are trying to control machines and people at the same time under the national mechanization plan, and hope to be able to manufacture their own parts as a foundation for manufacturing their own machines. After this goal is achieved, they will no longer have to buy marine engines and various parts from foreign countries, and will be able to be self-reliant and self-sufficient. Eliminating the Jiangxi Bandits - Absolutely Confident - Talk by Wan Guo'an After Inspecting the Front Lines

(Nanchang) Wan Guo'an, a nationalist literary writer, came to Jiangxi to join the army in the early spring of this year to participate in the suppression of bandits. He arrived in the province from the front lines on official business on the morning of the 14th. According to him, the Jiangxi bandits can be wiped out in the near future, and our army has absolute confidence. The bandit troops are familiar with the terrain and move quickly, often breaking up into small groups and then gathering them together, which makes us exhausted. However, since our army changed its strategy and implemented a steady and gradual advance, building bunkers everywhere, the bandits have been unable to do anything. If they break up into small groups, we can calmly defeat them one by one. If they gather the small groups together, then the main force is concentrated, which gives us a clear target and makes it easy to encircle them from all sides and wipe them out in one fell swoop. Moreover, the bandit side has a small number of strong men and a lack of guns and ammunition. All necessary supplies cannot be replenished due to our economic blockade. Therefore, in military terms, the bandits have become fish in a cauldron, and their elimination is only a matter of time. Every time our army recovers a place, in addition to constructing bunkers and other military fortifications, we build houses, cultivate fields, build roads, and plant trees for the people, so that the local area can recover and the people can live and work in peace. Therefore, the troops on the front lines are deeply trusted and loved by the people. The bewitching, deception, and intimidation that the bandits usually used on the people has now completely failed. The people in the bandit areas are in deep water and fire, and they deeply hope that the National Army will advance to relieve them, just like expecting clouds in a severe drought. (Central News Agency dispatch from the 14th)

Disposal Measures for Defaced National Currency

(Hankou) The Xingying recently ordered the headquarters of the three provinces to issue a seal of Soviet characters on the national currency by the Red bandits. It attempted to seal off the cash in the bandit areas, but since it collapsed and scattered among the people, it was inconvenient to allow them to use it, but it could not be weighed with counterfeit currency. Therefore, three measures are specified: (1) The hard currency shall be recovered by the local county government at a full price and transferred to the financial department of each province for appropriation and reimbursement, and the financial department shall prepare a document and transfer the original currency to the central currency factory for re-casting. (2) The paper currency shall be collected by the local county government at full price and transferred to the original issuing bank for cash redemption according to the face value. (3) The local military and political leaders should always strictly investigate the reasons for the defacement of the national currency and its source to prevent abuses. If there is any suspicion of collusion with the Red bandits, they should still be punished according to law. (Central News Agency dispatch from the 14th)

丨July 14th Reuters Special Commercial Telegram丨

Gold and Silver

The price of gold in London fell by half a penny this morning to 138 shillings. There was nothing special in the London silver market today, with little trading and stable popularity. Spot was 20 pence 625, down 0625. Futures were unchanged, remaining at 20 pence 6875.

The Bombay silver market was looser today, with evening futures at 57 rupees 4 annas for July, 57 rupees 5 annas for August, and 57 rupees 7 annas for September, all down 6 pounds compared to yesterday's closing price.

Exchange Rates

The foreign exchange market in the UK and the US this morning was still uninteresting and lacked vitality. The opening exchange rate between the UK and the US was 5 yuan 03875, the same as yesterday's closing price between the US and the UK. It fell 0625 at 11:00 am and rebounded 125 at noon, but the amount of the increase fell again at the close, so the final price was 5 yuan 038115, down 0625 from the opening.

The opening price between the UK and France was 7 francs 40, the same as yesterday's price, and remained unchanged until the close.

The opening exchange rate between the US and the UK this morning was the same as yesterday, remaining at 5 yuan 03875. The market was quiet, and the exchange rate did not change until 11:00 am.

Cotton and Wheat

New York Cotton The cotton market opened stable and active. The weather in Texas is still dry. Speculators bought in, but there were also profit-taking and sales from the South, which were absorbed. Some reports of fruit worm damage have been received, so the opening price rose by 5 pounds. It continued to rise after that. At 10:40 am, the price of cotton was up 45 pounds from the opening price.

Bombay Cotton The Bombay cotton market rose due to purchases by speculators and futures traders, but was slightly affected later due to sales by European exporters. The price of Bellocchi cotton for July and August was 216 rupees 25 this evening, up 2 rupees.

Liverpool Cotton Liverpool cotton prices continued to rise today. At the close, the October contract was up 9 pounds at 6.84.

Liverpool Wheat The Liverpool wheat market was firm this morning due to the stable Chicago wheat market yesterday. The closing price for the October contract was 5 shillings 2 pence 625, up one and a half pence.

Rubber

The London rubber market opened stable this morning. The trading price for October and December was 7 pence 25, up 0625 from yesterday.

Securities

The New York Stock Market opened sluggishly this morning with narrow trading. Stock prices mostly rose slightly, and market sentiment was stable. According to observers, although speculators are now leaning towards commodities again, causing a slight impact on the stock market, the strong footing after yesterday's slight rise indicates that stock prices will continue to gradually rise. Japanese Garrison Locks Down Our Northeastern Coastline in New York to Prevent Supply of Weapons to Volunteer Army, Stipulates Three Prevention Measures

An Dong Special Dispatch: In order to prevent ships supplying weapons to the triangular zone from our mainland from docking, the Japanese army has ordered the coastal police force to immediately arrest any suspicious ships and conduct strict searches. At the same time, it has urged the An Dong County Public Office to convene village chiefs from various coastal counties to discuss prevention measures, and three items have been decided, which will be implemented immediately: (1) Along the coast, a watchtower will be set up every three li, and self-defense team outposts will be set up inside to monitor nearby ships. (2) All dense reeds within 200 meters of the coast will be cut down. (3) The self-defense team on watch must immediately report directly to the coastal police force if they encounter any suspicious ships (Northeast News Agency).

Jiangsu Construction Department to Relieve Drought in Jiangnan, Proposes Plan to Draw Water from Rivers and Lakes, Project Cost Estimated at 450,000 Yuan, Uses Pumps to Draw Water into the Grand Canal

Zhenjiang Dispatch: The Jiangsu Construction Department believes that the waterways in Jiangnan counties are mainly based on the Grand Canal, and their water sources are either from the Yangtze River tide, which is irrigated from the river mouths, or from mountain water supported by lakes and ponds. In order to relieve the drought, it is proposed to draw water from both the river and the lake, and irrigate each water area connecting the river and the lake, and inject it into the Grand Canal, so that water can be used for bailing everywhere, benefiting everyone. The location, method, and cost of all pumping stations are stipulated as follows:

Pumping Locations: (1) Dantu Port in Zhenjiang, entering the canal from Dantu Port; (2) Jiuqu River Mouth in Danyang, entering the Danyang Canal from Jiuqu River Mouth; (3) Menghe in Wujin, entering the canal from Shiqiao Town to Benniu at the confluence of the large and small Menghe; (4) Desheng Port Mouth in Wujin, bailing water in Weicun Town, and entering the canal along Desheng Port; (5) Zao Port Mouth in Wujin, bailing water in Xutang Town, and dividing it into the canal through Fenghuang River and Yan Tang River; (6) The above six locations are for drawing river water; (7) Houxu Gehu Mouth in Wujin, bailing water into the canal; (8) Liaohe Gehu Mouth in Wujin, bailing water into Wujin Canal and Yichang Caohe; (9) Diaqiao Gehu Mouth in Wujin, bailing water into Wujin Canal; (10) Yixing Gaodu Port, injecting water from Gehu into Yichang Caohe and Yixing City; (11) Wuxi Quxi Mouth, entering Wuxi Canal from Taihu Lake; (12) Wuxian Wangting Shadun Port Mouth, entering the canal from Taihu Lake; (13) Wuxian Xukou, entering the Xujiang River to Suzhou City from Taihu Lake; (14) Wujiang Guajing Mouth, entering the canal from Taihu Lake; (15) Wujiang Beichi Dapu Mouth, from Taihu Lake.

Entering the canal; (16) Wuxian Weiting Yangcheng Lake Mouth entering Zhihe Pond, the above eleven locations are for drawing lake water.

Implementation Methods: (1) Regarding the determination of construction sites, allocation, installation of pumps, the Department of Construction will send personnel to guide the construction, and the local county government will be responsible for the management, and the Department of Construction will supervise it at any time. If the pumps cannot be prepared in time, fire engines and old-fashioned manual water wheels can be used as supplements. All county rice mills should also be borrowed to provide power for the pumps; (2) Regarding the distribution of bailing water into tributary rivers and fields, farmers should bail and save themselves, and the county government should be responsible for overall planning and distribution to avoid disputes, and send technicians to guide them at any time.

Budget Estimate and Resolution Method: Passed a special drought relief fund of 450,000 yuan as the project cost for drawing water from rivers and lakes. The Construction Department and the Finance Department will quickly handle it together.

Heavy Rain in Shaanxi Province, Yellow River Continues to Rise, Water Level Reaches Over 29 Meters

Jinan Correspondence: The water level of the Yellow River in Shandong has risen sharply due to heavy rain in the upstream Shaanxi Province. The huge waves and torrents poured fiercely into Shandong. The water level at Luokou has reached 28 meters and 3 inches. Zhang Lianjia, the Director of the Shandong River Affairs Bureau, was afraid that an accident would occur due to the sudden rise in water level, so he immediately notified the flood control personnel along the river to strictly guard against it to avoid negligence. The River Affairs Bureau received another report from Luokou in the middle reaches at 6:00 AM today (12th) that the water level suddenly rose sharply again, still due to the continuous rise in water in the upstream Shaanxi Province. Therefore, the water level in Shandong's various reaches has also increased sharply. Except for those that had fallen during the previous easing, it has risen sharply by 1 meter, 3 inches, and 6 minutes, which is equivalent to more than 4 feet in Chinese measurement, and the water level has reached 29 meters and 5 minutes. It is still more than 2 meters lower than the highest water level last year. By 12:00 noon, another report was received that the water level continued to rise by 8 minutes, and the total water level was 29 meters, 1 inch, and 3 minutes. It only eased and dropped 1 inch and 8 minutes at 6:00 PM. After receiving the report, Zhang Lianjia, the Director of the River Affairs Bureau, set off from Jinan at 6:00 AM today (12th) to inspect the rising water situation at Luokou in the middle reaches and to check the flood control works. He also sent separate telegrams to the flood control sections, etc., to strictly guard and patrol all night to avoid negligence, and reported the rising water situation to the provincial government. After inspecting the river defense and material factory at Luokou, Zhang returned to Jinan immediately.

Page 11

National Army Presses Towards Ningdu, Bandit Areas Can Be Fully Recovered Once Highway Is Completed

Nanchang Correspondence: After the National Army recaptured Guangchang, it immediately launched two columns to attack the bandit areas and capture Shicheng. According to Guangchang, the Northern Route Headquarters was moved from Fuzhou to Nancheng, and the General Headquarters, which was originally in Nancheng, also moved to Guangchang. General Commander Chen Cheng is currently serving as the deputy commander of the military training regiment in Lushan, and all military affairs are temporarily handled by Deputy General Commander Luo Zhuoying. Luo arrived in Guangchang on the 2nd of this month to command, and the morale of the front was greatly boosted. On the 3rd, they recaptured Toupi, Hucenba, and Dongshanba, the key passes to Ningdu, and the Yongfeng garrison also recovered Toupi, east of Longgang, and advanced to the Yuexi area, where the three counties of Yongning and Xing meet. The two highways from Guangchang to Ningdu and from Yongfeng Longgang to Guganglonggang in Xingguo are now under the protection of the army, advancing step by step towards the bandit areas. At the same time, the highway from Taihe on the west bank of the Gan River to Tingning in Fujian Province is also under construction. Once the highway is completed, the bandit areas can be fully recovered. The Department of Civil Affairs expects that the six counties of Ning, Shi, Rui, Ling, Hui, and Xing will be fully recovered within this year, but the post-war talent needed in the bandit areas is not easy to find. It has been submitted to the provincial government that all civil servants from the above six counties must follow the army to help with the post-war work in the counties. The post-war personnel from the nine counties sent by the governments of Jiangxi and Fujian provinces will also follow the army to work after completing their training. Therefore, the recovery of each district this time is by no means comparable to the previous situation where the bandits retreated when the soldiers arrived and returned when the soldiers left (10th).

Eastern Fujian Military Suppression Launched Against Bandits, Provincial Government Appoints Wang Jingjiu as Commander, Mei Pan Troops Begin Fierce Fighting with Bandits

Fuzhou Correspondence: Because of the rampant banditry along the coast of eastern Fujian, the Fujian Provincial Government ordered Wang Jingjiu, the commander of the 87th Division and the garrison commander of Fuzhou, to lead his troops to carry out a large-scale search and suppression within one month. After receiving the order, Wang led the personnel of the division headquarters to Ningde on July 6. The provincial government received Wang's telegram on the 8th, reporting that he had arrived safely in Ningde County. He plans to set up a bandit suppression headquarters in the county. After the arrangements are completed, he will convene the county magistrates of the eastern Fujian counties and the officers of the troops to hold a bandit suppression meeting to clarify the activities of the local bandits and the recent bandit suppression situation in order to decide on the suppression strategy. On the 10th, the provincial government received another telegram from Wang, stating that it has now been ascertained that the largest bandits in eastern Fujian are Ma Liefeng, Ren Tiefeng, Gao Chengxue, Chen Youbao, and Zeng Guanyu's wife, etc. Each gang has hundreds of people, calling themselves peasant armies or Red Guards. They have established pseudo-district Soviet governments in Zheyang, Zhexi Fuxi, Bailu, Chendun, Xiedun, Jinshan, Nancuo, and other places where the counties of Xiapu Fuan, Fuding, and Ningde meet. The pseudo-government is divided into departments such as finance, military affairs, transportation, culture, grain transportation, land equalization, and Dingfan. They also build blockhouses and mountain villages in strategic locations to defend themselves. On the one hand, they force the people to drive them, and on the other hand, they rob rice and salt to accumulate food. Recently, a group of red bandits, about 1,500 to 1,600 people, with more than 700 guns, has also been discovered in Meiyang Panxi, where the two counties of Ningde and Fuan meet. They looted everywhere, and the situation was especially rampant. Liu Anqi's brigade has been sent to Ningde to suppress them, and fierce fighting has begun. The other routes will be launched after the arrangements are clear (11th).

Northwestern Inspection Notes - Special Correspondent of This Newspaper, Geng Ya

Zhongwei Divides New County

On the 24th, we departed from Zaoyuan Fort and traveled ten li, passing by Guandi Temple. There is a primary school there. Mr. Xu approached and talked to the students, asking, "After studying, what career will you pursue?" They replied, "We will become district chiefs or village chiefs to serve the local area." At that time, the teacher returned from outside, looking flustered. He tugged at Mr. Xu's sleeve and repeatedly called, "Sir, please come to my house for a meal." Mr. Xu politely declined and inquired about the school's operation. He learned that the school has more than forty mu of school land, which can collect more than 320 yuan per year. There are two teachers, each of whom can earn a salary of more than 160 yuan per year. In addition to providing their own books and stationery, students must also pay tuition fees of three to five yuan. The textbooks they read are all the Three Character Classic, Hundred Family Surnames, Poems, and Books. After traveling fifteen li on a sandy road, we arrived at Xiayingzi. The soil is fertile and the water is good, better than Zaoyuan Fort. The vegetable gardens and date orchards are quite lush. Outside the village, green grass is everywhere, and women carry baskets and buckets to dig bitter vegetables or pick bean leaves for a living. The situation is very bleak. Several empty cars came towards us. When asked, they said that they were transporting goods from Ningxia Province to the south. When they arrived at the dam, they were forced to unload the goods by a certain unit, and their livestock were taken to transport wounded soldiers to Zhongwei without paying foot fees, so they returned empty.

[<i>Scenery of the Ningxia Tang Canal Dam</i>]

(See "Small Dam and Large Dam" on July 9)

After traveling forty li, we arrived at Shikong Fort. We rested for a while and met a催欵员 (debt collector) from the Ningxia Reclamation Bureau. We talked about the land survey. He said, "We will start with the five counties of Ningsuo, Jinji, Lingwu, Zhongwei, and Zhongning first, which is the first phase, and it must be completed by the end of August. The remaining counties are the second phase, which must be completed by the end of the year. The fees for registration, registration, and certificates are eight cents per mu. When the whole province is collected, it will be 300,000 to 400,000 yuan." There are many wolfberry gardens in Shikong Fort. Each mu can collect for eight years, and each plant can collect one sheng, which is very profitable. After traveling another twenty li, we arrived at Shengjing Pass. On the left, it leans against steep mountains, and on the right, it is next to river canals. In the past, it was a military stronghold, but now the pass is dilapidated and unbearable. Because of the hot weather, Mr. Du, Mr. Xu, and Mr. Luo took a bath in the river. Because the water there is very alkaline, it is excellent for removing dirt and cleansing the body. We arrived at Zhongwei County in the evening at 7:00 PM and stayed at Yuhua Hospital.

[<i>Leather Raft Used for Navigation on the Yellow River</i>]

(See "The Importance of Qing Tongxia" on July 10)

We stayed in Zhongwei County for three days, the 25th, 26th, and 27th. This is because the short-axle car used from Ningxia to Zhongwei needs to be replaced with a long axle to be suitable for going to Lanzhou. Moreover, there is a great lack of drinking water at each station from here on. On the 26th and 27th, Qinghai wounded soldiers set off, so we waited two more days to avoid each other. Both felt thirsty. On the afternoon of the 25th, we went to visit Gao Temple (i.e., Jade Emperor Pavilion). The contents are divided into pavilions for the Supreme God, the Five Mountains, the Three Purities and the Four Heavens, Wenchang Guandi, Guanyin, etc., with five or six floors. Each floor has seven bays, five bays, and three bays, for a total of no less than dozens of halls and pavilions. The structure is exquisite, the decoration is magnificent, the paintings are dark red, and the gold is brilliant. The atmosphere is consistent, and it is also rich in winding and tortuous details. Climbing high and looking into the distance, I am leisurely and fascinated. The headquarters of the 3rd Brigade of the 15th Route is stationed in the temple. I met the adjutant of the brigade. According to him, in order to maintain local customs, the division implemented a ban on prostitution and gambling. It once worked with the Public Security Bureau to investigate the household registration. There were three or four hundred well-known prostitutes in the city, all of whom were engaged in this flesh-and-blood career because of livelihood. However, there were also those who used this to win over powerful people in the military and political circles in order to say something and seek benefits in case of trouble. Later, after the adjutant informed the brigade commander, he agreed to meet us. We had a very pleasant conversation. The brigade commander, Ma Yingcai, is tall and has excellent spirits. He said, "I plan to establish a reading research association in the headquarters in the near future, so that soldiers and officers can study and learn from each other outside of academic and subject operations, so that their knowledge will not lag behind. For local public welfare undertakings, we will divide them into (1) repairing streets, (2) repairing city walls, (3) setting up public libraries, (4) running public schools, (5) building public sports fields. All work will be shared by officers and soldiers of the headquarters." Except for the public schools, which are still under preparation, all the matters described by Brigade Commander Ma are facts, which is truly commendable.

The epidemic is prevalent in the suburbs, and many people have died, because it is the hot summer weather and no attention is paid to public health. There is a great lack of medicines for infectious diseases such as cholera and typhoid fever, and it is difficult to treat those who suffer from them, and there is often a danger to life. The same is true for dysentery and diphtheria. According to Dr. Hu of Yuhua Hospital, "The above-mentioned diseases are prevalent once a year. Because they are internal medicine, patients do not often consult Western doctors, and Chinese medicine is also expensive and unaffordable. Many people die without medicine."

[<i>Tianxian Town in Qing Tongxia</i>]

(See "The Importance of Qing Tongxia" on July 10)

Zhongwei and Zhongning originally belonged to one county. Last year, the Provincial Government Department of Civil Affairs believed that the county had a vast area and a large rural area, and the county government could not reach local administration. Therefore, it suggested that the Provincial Committee divide the two counties. It was approved by the Provincial Affairs Meeting. Zhongwei will remain as it is, and the county seat of Zhongning County will be located in Ningan Fort. The current situation of the division of the two counties is recorded as follows:

Zhongwei County covers an area of 4,200 square li, 280 li from east to west and 150 li from north to south. It reaches Alashan in the north, Jinji in the southeast, Shengjing Pass and Shanhe Bridge, Jingyuan in the southwest, and Hongshui in the northwest. The arable land is about 1,200 square li, the sandy land accounts for about 1,800 square li, and the wasteland that can be reclaimed is still being measured. Agricultural products include rice, wheat, and poppies. The coal-producing areas include Daliang Mountain and the upper and lower reaches of the river. The annual output is about 4,550 tons (private mining is not included). Each ton is worth about 5.5 yuan. Unfortunately, it is mined manually, and the output is limited.

Zhongning County was established on January 1, 1934. The county covers an area of 1,500 square li, 150 li from east to west and 100 li from north to south. The arable land is about 950 square li, the sandy land is about 400 li, and the rest is the wasteland along the river. The county borders Jinji County in the east, Shengjing Pass in the west, Haiyuan in the south, Daba in the north, and Alashan in the northwest. In addition to miscellaneous grains and poppies, the county is most abundant in wolfberries. The annual output is about 1,500 dan (240 jin per dan). Each dou is worth 30 to 80 yuan. The best is called Zao Huang, 80 yuan per dou. The next is called Kui Yuan, 60 yuan per dou. The next is called Hui Huo (i.e., ordinary), 30 yuan per dou. Shikong Fort in the county produces about 2,000 tons of coal per year, and each ton is worth 5 to 6 yuan. The county produces more than 100 dan of black moss and more than 100 dan of licorice per year. The value of agricultural by-products throughout the year is no less than 300,000 yuan.

Zhongwei and Zhongning counties are known as rich areas in Ningxia, but the burden on farmers is too heavy, and the rural economy is still in a slump. According to farmers in Zhongwei and a section chief of the county government, the county government often employs more than a dozen催徵委員(tax collection commission members) and 60 county servants to be responsible for催款(tax collection) affairs in various townships. Each time the commission members and county servants go to the countryside to催款(collect taxes), the farmers must provide travel expenses and food. If they are not treated well, they will be insulted. At present, the burden on farmers is more than 9 yuan per person (average) per year. The journey from Zhongwei to Yingpanzi takes three days and is mostly sandy ridges. It is more difficult to travel than the Sichuan Road because the hooves sink and the wheels get stuck. Because the county government received a phone call from the Department of Civil Affairs, it hired a strong mule and sent two escorts. The kindness is very appreciated.

Gu Zhutong Urges All Sectors in Nancheng to Practice the New Life Movement

Nancheng Correspondence: Since the Northern Route Commander-in-Chief Gu Zhutong was stationed here, he has faithfully practiced the New Life Movement advocated by Chairman Chiang Kai-shek. In addition to organizing discipline squads to guide and supervise, organizing New Life Movement clubs to promote and repeatedly convening expanded memorial weeks to repeatedly publicize, he also convened meetings with leaders from all walks of life to discuss how to practice hygiene and cleanliness in order to transform the bad environment of Nancheng. It was resolved to invite hygiene experts to write tens of thousands of wall posters and slogans, distribute them inside and outside the city and in various townships for posting, and print multiple kinds of pamphlets and leaflets on hygiene for distribution. On the other hand, we requested the Jiangxi Department of Education to send 30 students from the Provincial Public Teacher Training Institute to Nancheng on the 7th, 8th, 9th, and 10th of June to carry out propaganda work. After the staff arrived, they were divided into ten groups and guided by the heads of the保甲(baojia) to promote the meaning of hygiene and cleanliness in the bustling streets inside and outside the city. We also invited twelve celebrities from the medical community to give lectures on the essentials of hygiene in the Sun Yat-sen Memorial Hall in the Twelfth Middle School in phases on the 10th and 11th of June. Party, government, military, and school leaders and保甲(baojia) leaders all participated, and the audience each day was about two to three thousand people, who were all moved. From the 12th to the 14th, a hygiene exhibition was held in the Tianyi Mountain Gospel Church, displaying various pictures about hygiene and physiology, so that the public could easily understand and improve. In the evening, hygiene films from the Lanterns and Inspirational Society were shown in the hall and the Twelfth Middle School to arouse public interest, with more than 10,000 people attending in an orderly manner. On the opening day, Gu personally attended the meeting to guide everything. From the 19th to the 21st, a city-wide cleaning was carried out. In addition to the automatic cleaning of each household and shop, all the streets and public places in the city were divided into three major sections, each of which was headed by the Tenth Administrative District Command, the Twentieth Route General Command, and the Commissioner's Office, with several officials leading 20 soldiers, 9 cleaners, and 9 garbage trucks, together with the 保甲(baojia) leaders, to take responsibility. Now the garbage piled up like mountains on the streets of the city has been cleaned up, and it has been completely renewed. From the 22nd to the 24th, door-to-door inspections of hygiene and cleanliness were conducted, and the best first, second, and third places were selected for awards to encourage them. The award ceremony was held on the small school grounds on the 29th, with 10,000 people attending. In order to prevent epidemics, Commander-in-Chief Gu ordered the military medical department of the headquarters to supervise the implementation of epidemic prevention injections and vaccinations by various public hospitals, and plans to extend the deadline to July 15 to achieve universal coverage, which is of great benefit to the people of Nancheng.

Mountain Kun: Disaster Prevention and Relief in the Midst of Severe Drought

Since February, Kun County has not seen a drop of rain. The river channels within the city walls are completely dry, making it quite difficult for residents to obtain drinking water. In the rural areas, the rice seedlings in the higher fields have withered and died completely, and those in the lower areas are also on the verge of collapse. Farmers are using oxen to draw water day and night, and there have been frequent reports of oxen collapsing from exhaustion. In response to public opinion, the county government has banned slaughtering for a week, and the populace has hung up banners everywhere praying for rain. However, the past two days have been exceptionally hot, and the heavens show no sign of rain. The price of rice has risen to twelve yuan and fifty cents per stone today, and there is still a tendency for it to continue to rise. Seeing that the drought is turning into a disaster, the landlords within the city held a meeting at the United Fire Relief Association yesterday afternoon at 1:00 PM to discuss drought relief. As a result, they submitted a request to the county government and telegraphed the provincial authorities to allocate and lend 80,000 yuan in silver from the county's remaining funds, and to borrow 40,000 yuan in silver from the Farmers Bank as an immediate emergency measure. The drought prevention measures are as follows: (1) Purchase water pumps; (2) Organize irrigation cooperatives; (3) Add draft cattle; (4) Open up Yuqianbanglou (a water source); (5) Subsidize farmers' water-drawing costs. The above measures require the full cooperation of the township heads and various tenants under the supervision of the Mountain District Office, and twenty-three people including Xu Menglin, the district officer, have been appointed to actively handle the matter.

[P Songjiang: Convicted Appellant Dies Tragically After Jumping From Train

The County Court sentenced Wang Bao Xiang, a bandit from Xiaokunshan, to sixteen years of imprisonment, and Gu Ada to eighteen years. Peng Xiaodi, Chen Xuesan, and Chen Ziping, perpetrators of the Fengjing Wutong Temple robbery case, were sentenced to three years and six months each. Each of them refused to accept the judgment and filed an appeal. Furthermore, Qian Sanbao, a counterfeiter, was sentenced to three months, and Qian Ahu and Sun A'er were each sentenced to two months. The prosecutor filed an appeal. The Jiangsu High Court scheduled a hearing. The prosecutor's office dispatched bailiffs Zhou Shaotang and Tao Jinhe to escort the above-mentioned criminals to Suzhou on the 14th at 10 AM. However, when the train passed Xinzhuang Station, about four miles east of Dongshan, Qian Ahu, the counterfeiter sentenced to two months, feigned needing to urinate, and taking advantage of the guards' inattention, jumped from the train to escape, tragically dying under the wheels. The bailiffs immediately reported to the prosecutor's office via long-distance telephone, and an official was dispatched to investigate.

Fire Brigade Trial Run Causes Misunderstanding

The members of the First District Fire Brigade in this city, considering the dry weather and to ensure preparedness for fire emergencies, announced that they would gather at Songhui Motor Road every day at 6:00 PM to practice with the pump trucks. Coincidentally, on the evening of the 12th, a slight disturbance arose at Songhui Amusement Park due to a ticket dispute. Three people, including Lu A'yun, were arrested on the spot for questioning. After investigation, it was determined that they were not related to the fire brigade members. Subsequently, in the "Daily Morning News" correspondence from this county, it was reported that fire brigade members and more than three hundred hooligans had disturbed the amusement park. The county magistrate, believing there was a background to it, is now thoroughly investigating. Upon reading the newspaper, all members of the First District believed the report was inaccurate and elected eight representatives to visit the county magistrate, presenting the "Daily Morning News." Magistrate Jin denied ever making such a statement on the spot, and said that the news item should be corrected immediately. The fire brigade members then expressed their satisfaction. They then visited the chief of the Public Security Bureau, who also agreed to issue a statement to clarify the matter. It is unknown whether the commotion can be resolved.

Suzhou: Relief Measures Amidst Severe Drought

The extreme drought and heat in Suzhou have been repeatedly reported in the "Suzhou News." Yesterday, the 14th, the scorching sun still blazed high, and the weather was hot and dry. In the rural fields, only thirty to forty percent of the land has been planted with seedlings. However, according to custom, even if rain comes after the third day of the sixth lunar month, it will be hopeless. Therefore, yesterday was nothing less than a death sentence for ordinary farmers. In addition to undertaking well-digging and other legitimate measures to alleviate the drinking water shortage, various local organizations in the urban area have been busy setting up altars and performing rituals to pray for rain. Furthermore, Director Wu of the Agricultural Implement Manufacturing Plant outside Xumen reported that all the water pumps in the plant have been sold out. He is now under provincial order to purchase two hundred more pumps without delay. Therefore, yesterday (the 14th), he went to Shanghai to purchase more, and has prepared 350,000 yuan in cash for the large-scale purchase of water pumps. Another 100,000 yuan will be used to purchase machinery parts and it is planned to convert various small wheel motors into water pumps, drawing water from Taihu Lake into the city. (Of the fifty-plus ferries traveling to various places, forty have ceased operation as of yesterday, the 14th.) This is to urgently alleviate Suzhou's water shortage. It is said that the Construction Department also dispatched personnel to Wuxi yesterday (the 14th) to survey the water situation in Taihu Lake, so that dams can be built in Taihu Lake, and then water can be pumped into various lakes and harbors. Because Taihu Lake is drying up, whether the above plan can be effective will be determined after a timely survey. At the same time, the Wu County Construction Bureau has decided to start opening artesian wells in the city at Pingjiang Road, Xinxueqian, Henggang, and Qimen. The county government has instructed the Chamber of Commerce to ban the hoarding of rice in order to stabilize market prices. As for the rice straw needed for residents' daily fuel, the source has already been cut off. Only 150 catties are sold per yuan. If there is no rain in another two days, it will be difficult for manure boats to enter the city, and residents' waste disposal may also become a problem.

Haimen: River Dredging Leads to Armed Conflict

The Xitou canal in the Third District, about ten miles long from north to south, is an important waterway in the district. Due to the prolonged drought and lack of rain, the canal has dried up. Residents, facing a drinking water shortage, elected representatives such as Yang Yunhe to petition the county government to allow them to open the canal themselves to connect to the Yangtze River in order to draw in the tide. Yesterday (the 12th), more than a thousand villagers took action. Unexpectedly, villagers in the northern section of the canal suddenly expressed opposition, gathering more than a thousand people to stop them. The two sides clashed, using farm implements as weapons and engaging in a mixed battle. As a result, dozens of people on both sides were injured. Today (the 13th), each side submitted a complaint to the county government, and the villagers who were injured carried the Yang villager to the county to request an investigation.

Derelict Iron Barge Found in Songji Port

A derelict iron barge was washed ashore by a huge tide in the Songji Port beach in the First District the day before yesterday. The barge is of considerable size, with nothing inside. The local residents reported it to Xu Guozhang, the captain of the First Detachment of the Harbor Water Police, who sent police to guard the vessel and await the owner to claim it.

Wuxi: Crop Wilting, Disaster Imminent

Due to the drought and lack of rain, crops are wilting and disaster is imminent. Rice prices have risen, exceeding the eleven-yuan mark, and the poor who struggle daily for sustenance are crying out in distress. According to rice merchants, if it doesn't rain again, high-quality white japonica rice may reach sixteen yuan per picul. At 4:00 PM on the 13th, there was a sudden heavy rainfall. Henglin and Qishu Yan received four inches of rain. Qianzhou, Yuqi, and Beiqifang received an inch or so of rain. No raindrops fell in Bashi Bridge, Zhangjing Bridge, and Anzhen in the northern countryside, causing great disappointment to the villagers. Due to the canal drying up, inland ferries have been unable to operate and have all ceased operations since yesterday. Currently, farmers in various districts are finding their own remedies, building dams, dredging rivers, and cooperating in water pumping. Regarding the urban canals, the First District Office has decided to build three dams at the west, north, and south water gates and a water gate at the east gate, using electric power to pump water into the city from the west gate. In the future, ships transporting manure and fuel will be transshipped inside and outside the dams. However, city residents such as Zou Tongyi have raised objections, arguing that the water inside the dam is stagnant and that drinking it may be detrimental to hygiene, and that traffic will be permanently cut off. Therefore, they have sent a letter to the First District Chief Qian Zhongliang requesting a temporary delay in implementation. Yesterday (the 14th), the weather was slightly cooler, but epidemics were rampant and hospitals were very busy. People on the road often suffered from heatstroke, a phenomenon unseen in decades.

You Yinzhao and Others Abducted in Xinjiang

You Yin, the second son of the local gentry You Tong (Gan Chen), Zhao (Zi Ming Yizhao, currently a chief engineer at the Mechanical Department of the Ping Sui Railway), graduated with a bachelor's degree in civil engineering from Nanyang University and a master's degree in civil engineering from Cornell University in the United States. He previously served as an engineer for the Jing Sui Railway and Bei Ning Railway and was noted for his work at the Shanhaiguan factory on planning the reinforcement of bridges along the entire railway and implementing the project. Last autumn, the Ministry of Railways assigned him and Long Jicheng to accompany the world-renowned Swedish scientific explorer Sven Hedin and astronomer Chen Zongqi, along with nine others, to Mongolia and Xinjiang to survey the route of the Northwest Highway. While traveling from Suiyuan to Baiairulai, he sent a daily diary back to Xishan. After sending two letters from Hami this spring on February 11, there was no further news. Later, it was learned that he was detained by Ma Zhongying's troops, with his hands tied behind his back and a gun pressed against his chest, almost to the point of danger. On the sixth of this month, You again entrusted a friend to send a telegram from Moscow to his younger brother Xun Zhao (currently a technical officer in the Nanjing Municipal Government), stating that Yin and the entire team were safe. However, the "North China Daily News" in Shanghai recently reported via telegram from Peiping that the group of nine had been abducted again by Ma Zhongying's former troops and taken to Aksu. Upon hearing the news, his father, You Tong, and his relatives were extremely worried.

Leashed Female Corpse Found in River

A nameless female corpse, approximately twenty years old, was found the day before yesterday in the Liujiaqiao Canal in Santang Township near Ouqiao in the Fourth District. The upper body was naked, with only a bib, and the lower body was wearing black shorts, a silk belt, white stockings, and black shoes, appearing modern. The neighborhood chief, Chen Wenyuan, reported it to the local sub-court. Prosecutor Shen led officials to conduct an on-site examination. The corpse's neck had two deep marks from hemp rope. Both hands were tied behind the back, and a millstone was tied to the back. Large stones were also tied around the waist and feet. There was no water in the abdomen, and no mud or sand in the fingernails or nostrils. It was determined that she had been strangled to death before being dumped into the river. Because no family was found, the chief was instructed to provide a coffin and burial, and to wait for the arrest of the perpetrator and further investigation. Furthermore, in the Zizania latifolia fields near Xujiang on Xingxiang Bridge, No. 596, in Bodugang, outside the South Gate, the field owner, Sheng Quan, recently installed an electric fence to deter badger damage. The other day, Zhou Jinbao's thirteen-year-old second son, A'er, from the same area, was wandering there and accidentally touched the electric fence and died. After neighborhood chief Deng Jiliang reported it to the local sub-court, Prosecutor Ren was dispatched to conduct an on-site examination and then collect the corpse. The boy's father, Zhou Jinbao, cried bitterly. The Public Security Bureau's Third Branch dispatched police to detain the field owner Zhang Shengquan and Cao Jinyuan and bring them to the court for questioning.

Swarms of Locusts Found in Northeast Countryside

Swarms of locusts have been found in the fields in the Zhouxiang area of the Shangshan Mountains, three miles from Anzhen in the northeast countryside of Wuxi, spreading for dozens of miles. Villagers are currently engaged in catching them and have reported to the county government for handling.

Changshu: Eastern Countryside Rejoices at the Downpour

Due to the prolonged drought, people were anxious. Local gentry, in order to reassure the public, in addition to worshiping the Dragon King to pray for rain, set up a Bagua formation in the Hui Ri Temple on the 13th, inviting monks and Taoists to chant scriptures and pray for rain. County Magistrate Zhou Heng has also been visiting various rural districts with the district chiefs to inspect the drought situation and personally persuade farmers to work hard at cultivation. If it is absolutely impossible, the county will provide seeds for replanting green beans. On the afternoon of the 13th, dark clouds suddenly gathered, and residents in the urban area hoped for rain, but it did not fall by the evening. According to reports from Meili Hecun, Tangqiao, Zhao City, and Dongbang and other villages, there was a sudden downpour at 1:00 PM, delighting the farmers. However, the temperature remained high, reaching 104.5 degrees, an all-time high in decades.

Wujiang: Model Widow's Sacrifice for Her Husband in Yanmu Town

Shi Hongfa, who ran a wine shop on South Street in Yanmu Town, Wujiang County, remarried Zheng, a woman from a nearby village, as his wife in the third month of the lunar calendar this spring. The couple got along quite well. However, Shi suddenly fell ill and died the day before yesterday. Zheng wailed and grieved excessively, saying that she would follow her husband to the afterlife. Relatives and children thought it was just a momentary expression of grief, a common reaction, so they gave some words of comfort.

Without any precautionary measures, Zheng changed her clothes, bathed, and hanged herself on the bed. By the time the family rescued her, she had been dead for a long time. The two corpses were displayed side by side, and a funeral was held. Local people believe that Zheng's chastity and martyrdom are worthy of praise and plan to request an honorific.

Nantong: Raising Funds to Build Dikes to Protect Against Collapse

The collapse of the Nantong riverbank is becoming more severe. The Nantong District Commissioner's Office has ordered the Construction Bureau to quickly implement protection works against collapse. After surveying, it has been decided to first build stone dikes at Langshan, Pingchao, Yaogang, and the Nantong riverbank, requiring 100,000 yuan, which is currently being raised.

Student Army Exercises Night Combat and Imposes Curfew

The Nantong summer student army will conduct night combat exercises and impose a curfew in Tongcheng from 8:00 PM on the 14th to 1:00 AM on the 15th. The Security Headquarters has issued a special notice to the public to avoid misunderstandings.

Zhenjiang: Eighty-Year-Old Man Drowns Himself in the River

Ding Kaitai, 77 years old, lived at No. 56 Dajiao Yang. Due to financial difficulties, he suddenly became world-weary. Taking advantage of his family's inattention, he drowned himself in the river at the Guanyin Nunnery on the edge of Ganlu Temple at 7:00 PM on the 11th. On the morning of the 12th, the family went to the Jiaoshan Life-Saving Bureau to register and request a search. The bureau immediately sent the No. 7 Red Boat, stationed at Ganlu Temple, to make efforts to search. Ding's body was recovered on the evening of the 12th. People were immediately notified to inform the deceased's family and the Ganlu Temple neighborhood security to report to the local court for legal examination and collection of the body for burial.

Zhenyi Will Open a Cooling Ferry

Since the beginning of summer, the weather has been dry and hot, a phenomenon not seen in decades. Ladies and gentlemen are wandering in the heat wave, feeling restless. Although Zhenyi has famous cooling spots such as Jinjiao Ganlu and the southern suburbs, the traffic is difficult to popularize, and each trip is too expensive, beyond the financial means of most people. In view of this, the Jiangsu Provincial Highway Administration has leased a small ferry from the Fu Transport Bureau and converted it into a cooling ferry, which will be moored at the Fuyun Pier, Zhongzheng Road Pier, Ganlu Temple, and Jiaoshan. This is entirely for the happiness of the people of the provincial capital, so the price is very low. It is said that the round trip from Fuyun Pier to Jiaoshan will only cost half a yuan per person, and other stations will cost a dime or a few cents. It is scheduled to officially open on the 21st of this month.

Jiashan: County Government Strictly Prohibits Raising Rice Prices

Rice hoarding in the county has almost been exhausted, while farmers have long been reduced to poverty, unable to make ends meet. As a result, rice prices have risen particularly sharply. In the middle of last month, the highest price for winter rice was only seven yuan and forty cents per picul, but now it has gradually increased. As of yesterday, each picul had reached about eight yuan and sixty cents. If it does not rain again, the autumn harvest will be hopeless, and rice prices will continue to rise. The county government issued a notice yesterday strictly prohibiting rice merchants from taking advantage of this drought disaster to raise rice prices and affect the people's food supply, and ordered the Rice Industry Association to jointly investigate and prohibit violations, which will be severely punished.

Yangzhou: Hot Weather and Cholera Epidemic

The weather in Yangzhou has been extremely hot for the past twenty days. It is so hot that one cannot breathe at noon, and one cannot sleep even at night, resulting in the emergence of general acute infectious diseases. According to a recent three-day survey, more than forty people in a corner of the city have died from cholera within two or three hours, most of whom are coolies. If it does not rain again in another five days, not only will epidemics spread, but the drinking water supply in towns and villages far from the canal will also become a problem. As for agricultural harvests, that is no longer a matter for immediate concern.

Gaoyou: Rampant Banditry in the Ninth District

The ninth district of the county has been plagued by bandits for years, and the farmers are suffering greatly. Last year, bandit gangs caused the most damage. After the county government dispatched teams to garrison Xuguangzhuang and other places to hold them, there were no traces of bandits. The other day, Director Xiang of the Provincial Security Office visited You to inspect the police force. The local police force was ordered to return to the city, but the bandits returned, looting the residents of Anjisi and Gengtianzhuang, and kidnapped Mu Rugan of Mujiazhuang, demanding a ransom of 2,000 yuan. They also set fire to several oil shacks.

Youlin Merchant Ship Looted by Bandits

The Youlin merchant ship departed from the city for Linze the day before yesterday. However, when it reached the Wuwen Port area of the Fourth District, it was suddenly ambushed by more than ten bandits who fired shots to warn and ordered it to stop. The bandits jumped aboard the merchant ship and searched it thoroughly. No passengers were spared, and all silver, goods, and cargo were looted. Before leaving, they also kidnapped the passenger Ding Deming and fled to the southeast.

Hot Weather and Rising Rice Prices

Since the beginning of summer, there has been little rainfall in the county. After half an inch of rain at the end of last month, it has not rained for many days, causing great damage to crops in the countryside. As a result, rice mills in the city arbitrarily raised rice prices. Superior rice rose from 7.2 yuan to 9.8 yuan, medium rice from 6.4 yuan to 8.6 yuan, and inferior rice from 5.8 yuan to 8 yuan. The general public was alarmed. If it does not rain again, rice prices will continue to rise.

Jingjiang: Tian Zhangshi Murders Her Husband

In Baimuqiao West Street, Sixth District, there is Tian Daguan, 52 years old, who married Zhang, who is 51 years old. Daguan's father, Bao Jiayun, died early, and his mother, Geng, remarried Tang Futing from Taixing (now 71 years old), who runs the Taihe Heng dyeing workshop to make a living. In 1923, Daguan was arrested and imprisoned for robbery and sentenced to 15 years in prison. He was released this spring after the National Government issued a general pardon, reducing his sentence by one-third. After returning home, he was at odds with his stepfather Tang Futing, his wife Zhang, and his daughter-in-law Lu, and conflicts often arose. He even threatened to kill his wife and daughter-in-law and burn down the house. His wife, terrified, decided to strike first. Yesterday late at night, taking advantage of Daguan's drunken sleep, she strangled him to death with a piece of white cloth. The neighbors discovered this and reported it to the town guard Mao Sen, who put the suspect under surveillance. A preliminary examination was conducted by Investigator Bao Chengshen. The main suspect, Tian Zhangshi, and accomplices Tang Futing, Tian Lu, and Lu Mingqing were all taken into custody for interrogation.

County Government Issues Arrest Warrant for Shen Hualong

Shen Hualong, the former captain of the 16th Water Police Brigade, was caught transporting opium in our county, along with three members of the team: Xi Hongsheng, Zhang Fengwu, and Wang Bingsheng, who were sentenced in the case. Later, Mei Xian accused Shen Hualong in a complaint to the county government.

Because he has repeatedly failed to appear after being summoned, an arrest warrant has been issued.

Cixi: Meteorite Falls Amidst Severe Drought

At about 9:00 PM the other day, a strange star suddenly appeared in the eastern sky of our county. It was as big as a small bowl, with a black shadow in the center and radiating light, flickering and unsteady. Its brightness was stronger than ordinary stars. Because it was still early, most people enjoying the cool air saw it. It lasted for about seven or eight minutes and then suddenly fell and disappeared. People discussed it a lot. Some said it was a drought demon star descending, a harbinger of drought and famine. An old farmer named Zhou spoke even more emphatically, saying that this star had fallen once in a certain year during the Qing Dynasty, and that year was a great drought. This year, it hasn't rained for a long time, and this star has descended again. We will record this and await the research of scientists.

Hangzhou: Severe Drought in Mogan Mountain Causes Drinking Water Problems

Recently, the weather has been hot, and the number of people going to Mogan Mountain to escape the heat has reached 4,500, and many more are going up the mountain every day. However, due to the lack of rain, the water source has been greatly reduced. The water needed by residents in Gangtou and Yinshan Heng is taken from the two water pipes in Luhuadang. Coolies carry buckets of water and trudge along the rugged mountain paths, working hard in the scorching heat. They flock to that place to fetch water, scrambling to be first. If it doesn't rain again, and the number of people going to the mountains to escape the heat continues to increase, the future is worrying.

Local News: Kong Xiangxi Explains the New Tariff Rules: Revised Cautiously After Careful Study by Experts; Impressed by this Trip to Inspect Various Provinces

Central News Agency reports: Finance Minister Kong Xiangxi arrived in Shanghai by plane on the evening of the 13th. Officials and staff of the Finance Ministry's Shanghai offices visited his private residence on the morning of the 14th to report. At 9:30, Kong went to the Central Bank to handle official business. Around 11:00, he met with reporters from various newspapers and made the following statement:

Inspecting the Finances of Various Provinces

According to Kong, he was very impressed by his trip to inspect the finances of the various provinces in North China, and he was especially pleased with the goodwill of the people towards the government. Due to the urgency of time, he was unable to personally inspect the border provinces such as Suiyuan, which he regretted. However, in order to understand the details of the various provinces, he dispatched personnel to inspect the places he had not personally visited, so as to know the details for reference in reform. The financial authorities of the various provinces and cities in North China were able to make efforts to implement the cases resolved at the National Financial Conference, which was gratifying. As for the abolition of various kinds of miscellaneous taxes in the provinces and cities, which has been officially implemented since July 1, many have been abolished, and it is expected that they can be completely abolished in a short period of time. Kong also said that the number of various kinds of miscellaneous taxes in the provinces and cities is countless. In Shanxi Province alone, more than 6 million yuan of miscellaneous taxes can be abolished annually, reducing the burden on the people.

Revising Import Tariffs

The new tariff rules promulgated by the Ministry of Finance

Have caused misunderstandings among some businessmen who have requested amendments. It has also been reported that

Some businessmen in Shanghai will send representatives to Beijing to petition him. If this is true, he should explain in detail to dispel doubts and to let people know the Ministry of Finance's caution in revising the tariff rules. Kong continued, saying that the revision of these new tariff rules had been carefully studied by Chinese and foreign experts for as long as six months, and the Ministry of Finance had revised them as many as four times. After the Ministry of Finance made a decision, it was submitted to the Executive Yuan for approval, and then to the Central Political Conference for review and approval before promulgation. He believes that these new tariff rules can take into account the interests of all parties. As for the increase in tariffs on machinery in the new tariff rules, it is because our country was previously unable to manufacture its own machinery, but now it is gradually able to do so, so the tariffs are increased to provide protection. As for printed fabrics, a type of cotton textile, because our country does not produce them, the tariffs have been reduced appropriately. All such increases and decreases are very reasonable.

Rescuing the Rong Family's Factories

Finally, Kong said that he likes to travel by nature and has visited the Yangtze River and North China in recent years, so he has decided to visit South China when he has some free time in government affairs, but the travel date has not yet been determined. As for the factories run by Rong Zongjing, a giant flour merchant, the government has decided to provide relief, and at a minimum, it will not allow them to shut down. He has just returned from North China and does not yet know the details of the factory's situation and the government's relief measures. Kong plans to stay in Shanghai for a week before returning to Beijing.

Telephone Service Between Zhejiang and Shanghai to Begin Tomorrow; Regulations Promulgated

According to Heping News Agency, with the exception of Nanjing, long-distance telephone service between Jiangsu and Zhejiang provinces, connecting neighboring provinces, is generally lacking. As Shanghai's telephone service is managed by the Ministry of Communications, it currently only extends to Hangzhou. To facilitate long-distance telephone service between various locations in Zhejiang Province and neighboring provinces, the Provincial Telephone Bureau and the relevant authorities have agreed on mutually beneficial measures for telephone and telegraph communication. It has now been decided that starting tomorrow (the 16th), Shanghai will begin providing telephone service to various locations in Zhejiang Province. New rates are being drafted and will be announced soon. Simultaneously, the Provincial Telephone Bureau will begin accepting and forwarding telegrams. Yesterday, the Provincial Telephone Bureau issued instructions to its local branches regarding the procedures for handling telephone service between Zhejiang Province and Shanghai, to be implemented starting on the 16th of this month. These procedures are outlined below: (1) Registered users of local telephones in Hangzhou and other cities in Zhejiang Province can connect to Shanghai long-distance service through their local telephone. (2) Those who purchase retail telephone tickets from the Zhejiang Provincial Telephone Bureau and its branches (hereinafter referred to as "Provincial Bureau") can connect to Shanghai long-distance service through retail telephones or designated local telephones. (3) The duration of calls between Shanghai and Zhejiang is measured in units of five minutes or less, starting from the time the called party answers. Calls lasting more than five minutes but up to ten minutes will be counted as two units. Continuous calls are limited to two units. (4) For long-distance calls from the Provincial Bureau to Shanghai or from Shanghai to the Provincial Bureau, the called party must have a local telephone. Calls will not be made to parties without a telephone. (5) The charges for calls between Shanghai and Zhejiang will be calculated as follows: Hangzhou to Shanghai County will be charged according to the established rates. All other lines of the Provincial Bureau will be charged according to the Provincial Bureau's established rates. (6)

For the Feng-Hang line and other bureaus, with the exception of Hangzhou and the Jia-Wu line bureaus, all calls to and from Shanghai will be relayed through the Jiaxing branch line. The rates for the Shanghai-Jiaxing segment will be charged according to the Ministry of Communications regulations, while the remaining segments will be charged according to the Provincial Bureau's regulations. (7) The Ministry of Communications' Shanghai-Hangzhou long-distance trunk line's charges and other procedures for the above telephone services will be handled according to the provisions of these measures, unless otherwise specified herein, and otherwise according to the Ministry of Communications' General Rules for Long-Distance Telephone Service. (8) Both parties shall meticulously record the number of calls and charges, and the Shanghai Telephone Bureau of the Ministry of Communications and the Zhejiang Provincial Telephone Bureau shall reconcile and settle accounts monthly. Detailed procedures shall be formulated through mutual consultation and submitted for approval. (9) These measures shall take effect on July 16, 1934. Matters not covered herein may be amended through mutual consultation.

Unexpectedly, while sailing to the Huangsang Estuary in Qizhou, the steel cable towing the "Puyi" broke suddenly, almost causing a major disaster. The "Jianguo" quickly released the "Puyi," resulting in it running aground for the second time.

French Community Celebrates National Day Yesterday; Mayor Wu and Others Attend

Yesterday marked the 145th anniversary of the French Republic. The French community in Shanghai, including officials, merchants, and people from all walks of life, held a grand celebration. In particular, Avenue Edward VII and Avenue Joffre were resplendent with a dazzling array of colors. Near Avenue Joffre, the huge lantern towers and arches in the style of ancient Chinese architecture at Route Cardinal Mercier, Rue Amiral Courbet, and Avenue de l'Eglise, attracted tourists and caused overcrowding. In addition, searchlights were shone from French warships, illuminating the entire area.

Shanghai Municipal Government Bonds to Be Available for Subscription Starting the 17th; Denominations of 100, 1,000, and 5,000 Yuan; Weekly Interest Rate of 7%; Interest Paid Semi-Annually; Underwritten by the Bank of China and Issued at 98

The Shanghai Municipal Government, for the purpose of improving roads and bridges, constructing museums, libraries, hospitals, sports fields, and slaughterhouses, and improving the Zhabei District and the city center, has been approved by the National Government to issue 3.5 million yuan in Shanghai Municipal Government Bonds. The bond certificates have been printed, and the underwriting has been entrusted to the Banque Franco-Chinoise. Subscriptions will begin at the Bank of China at 10:00 AM on the 17th of this month. Details are as follows:

Denominations and Guarantee

The total amount of the Shanghai Municipal Government Bonds for the 23rd year of the Republic of China is 3.5 million yuan. The bond certificates have been printed and are in unregistered form, with denominations of 100, 1,000, and 5,000 yuan. The 100 yuan denomination will be issued at 98 (plus interest from June 30th to July 17th). The weekly interest rate is 7%, payable semi-annually on December 31st and June 30th. In addition to the unconditional guarantee of the Shanghai Municipal Government, the license fees for automobiles, freight vehicles, motorcycles, and bicycles will serve as the primary collateral for the bonds until the principal and interest are fully repaid.

Issuance Procedures

The issuance procedures for the bonds have been finalized between the Municipal Government and the underwriting syndicate, the Banque Franco-Chinoise. It has been decided that subscriptions will begin at the Bank of China at 10:00 AM on the 17th of this month (Tuesday) and will close at or before 12:00 PM. Subscribers must pay the full amount at the time of subscription to receive a bank receipt. If there is no allocation, the full amount will be returned, as evidenced by the bank receipt. If the allocated amount is only a portion of the subscribed amount, a proportional refund will be given. Furthermore, for those handled by brokers from the Shanghai General Chamber of Commerce, the broker will receive a commission of 0.25% of the allocated amount as preferential treatment. Application forms can be obtained from the Bank of China, Zhejiang Industrial Bank, Wan Gu Savings Society, the Banque Franco-Chinoise, and other locations.

Redemption Method

The bonds will be redeemed annually by lottery at face value. The first redemption will be held on June 30th of the 24th year of the Republic of China. Interest will be paid semi-annually, with the first interest coupon due on December 31st of the 23rd year of the Republic of China. The bonds will mature in the 35th year of the Republic of China. The payment of due interest coupons and winning lottery tickets will be handled by the Bank of China, Central Bank of China, and Bank of Communications. However, the payment of principal and interest may be made at the discretion of the Shanghai Municipal Government, either in Bank of China notes, Shanghai Mint bars, or silver bars commonly used in international commerce. Regardless of the form of payment, each silver yuan payable to the bondholder must be equivalent to 23.493448 grams of pure silver. If payment is made in other currencies, the weight of pure silver must be equal to the amount of pure silver contained in the silver yuan payable. However, if commercial silver bars or currencies not commonly used in Shanghai are used for payment, a melting fee equivalent to the Shanghai Mint's legal rate at the time must be added.

Entrusted Custody

The use of the bond proceeds will be guided by a committee composed of the Director of the Shanghai Municipal Finance Bureau (Chairman), the Director of the Bureau of Public Works, the Director of the Bureau of Education, the Chairman of the National Debt Fund Management Committee, representatives of the Provisional Municipal Council, representatives of the Bank of China Association, and representatives of the Banque Franco-Chinoise. To protect the interests of the bondholders and facilitate the repayment of the principal and interest on the bonds, the underwriting syndicate has entrusted the National Debt Fund Management Committee to collect the license fees for automobiles and other vehicles from the agencies under the Shanghai Municipal Government and to hold them in trust for the repayment of the principal and interest on the bonds.

Military and Police Agencies Strictly Prohibit Riding Without Tickets; Garrison Command and Public Security Bureau Issue Notices; China General Omnibus Company Offers Preferential Treatment to Military and Police

The China General Omnibus Company of Nanshi, in order to facilitate public transportation and business, has found that soldiers and public officials ride without tickets, resulting in significant financial losses. The company has petitioned the Songhu Garrison Commander and the Shanghai Public Security Bureau to reiterate the prohibition and issue notices to be posted inside the buses, strictly prohibiting riding without tickets. Fearing that some may still refuse to purchase tickets, the 2nd Regiment of the Shanghai Garrison has dispatched military police, and the Municipal Public Security Bureau has assigned inspectors to travel on the buses of the China General Omnibus Company starting on the 16th of this month to enforce the regulations and maintain order. The texts of the notices from the military and police authorities are as follows: (1) Notice from the Songhu Garrison Command: For the purpose of issuing a notice, the China General Omnibus Company has petitioned for the issuance of a notice prohibiting soldiers from riding without tickets and has proposed preferential treatment for soldiers, allowing soldiers in uniform with insignia to ride in second-class carriages at half price. After review, it is deemed feasible. Therefore, this notice is issued. Hereafter, soldiers riding the bus must comply with the above regulations and purchase half-price tickets to alleviate the financial difficulties of the company and are not allowed to ride without tickets. Those who dare to violate this will be severely punished. This notice is issued by Commander Wu Tiecheng. (2) Notice from the Shanghai Public Security Bureau: For the purpose of issuing a notice, the China General Omnibus Company has petitioned for the issuance of a notice prohibiting public officials from riding without tickets to maintain traffic and business. Based on the aforementioned petition, in addition to the instructions, this notice is issued to all officers, who must comply. Those who dare to violate this will be severely punished.
