Municipal Committee in Each District Urgently Requests the Municipal Government to Protect Human Rights; People's Lawsuits Should First Investigate the Original Plaintiff

The municipal committee members of each district of Shanghai, Yang Xinzheng, Chen Tianxi, Wang Hui, Zhang Qiwen, Pan Hongding, Wu Xuen, Gu Shanzhang, Tang Chengzong, Zhu Jiajun, Zhu Zongluo, Zhou Nianzu, Ling Zhibin, Hong Lanxiang, Wang Shouyu, and others, jointly petitioned the municipal government and the garrison headquarters yesterday to prevent the filing of false accusations by first investigating the original plaintiffs in lawsuits. The original text is as follows: "It is an established rule that those who commit crimes among the people should be thoroughly investigated if they are reported. This is not only a fundamental principle in countries that value the rule of law, but also a crucial aspect for those who seek to achieve clear and just governance throughout history and across different countries. However, in these degenerate times, social morals have declined, and people's hearts have become treacherous, leading to situations where investigation is simply impossible. Even a slight grudge can lead to false accusations. Insidious individuals often use anonymous postings as tools for attack, while ruthless individuals do not hesitate to plant evidence or engage in slanderous accusations. Government agencies aim to eliminate evil and must conduct thorough investigations, but they may inadvertently fall into traps set by cunning individuals. By the time the truth is revealed, the physical freedom, property, and reputation of the accused have already suffered immeasurable damage. If grievances cannot be redressed and right cannot be distinguished from wrong, the situation becomes increasingly hopeless, and injustices sink to the bottom of the sea. Although our country's constitution is still being drafted, the provisional constitution has long guaranteed the people's freedom of person, residence, and property, and stipulates that punishment or unlawful arrest should not be imposed except in accordance with the law. This is essential to protect the people's rights and interests. The late Dr. Sun Yat-sen repeatedly emphasized the importance of people's rights in his Three Principles of the People. As we focus on the rule of law, implement the Three Principles of the People, and transition from political tutelage to constitutional governance, how can we neglect the people's rights and interests? Chairman Chiang Kai-shek has issued a directive to all regions, requiring that people's accusations against officials be based on solid evidence. By extension, mutual accusations among the people must also be based on solid evidence. Otherwise, those who are eager to cause trouble will excel at framing others, and anonymous postings will proliferate everywhere. Fortunately, if the government does not investigate, the senders of these postings will suffer no harm. However, if the government investigates based on these postings, the accused may be summoned, detained, or even have their homes searched and their reputations ruined, suffering undue harm. Imagine someone being falsely accused of selling or consuming morphine. If a bag of lime or powder is found in their home, it cannot be identified immediately and can only be confirmed after the case is investigated or analyzed. Before the verdict is reached, it is difficult to release the accused. What is the extent of their physical and mental suffering? Similarly, falsely reporting banditry or communism can be terrifying. If the person who framed the accused can be found, they can be punished for making a false accusation, even if the accused has suffered temporary pain. Otherwise, even if the case is resolved, how will the accused be compensated for their suffering? This will only embolden troublemakers and make everyone feel insecure. In light of this, and for the sake of protecting the people's rights and interests, the committee members dare to offer their heartfelt words. We earnestly request that you order the Public Security Bureau to first investigate the original plaintiffs in lawsuits. If the accusations are not false, then accept the case to prevent cunning individuals from harming the innocent and protecting the good. We humbly await your command."

Cotton Control Association Bans Watering of Cotton: Fourteen Rules Issued Yesterday

After the Cotton Control Association received the Ministry of Industry's notice on fourteen rules banning the watering of cotton yesterday, it immediately ordered the Cotton Trade Association to comply. The rules are as follows: Rule 1: The legal standard for water content in domestic cotton is 11%. Rule 2: The maximum water content in domestic cotton sold on the market is 13%. Rule 3: The sale of domestic cotton with water content exceeding the maximum limit is strictly prohibited. Rule 4: Those who intentionally water or adulterate cotton with the intention of gaining illegal profits shall be sentenced to imprisonment for up to three years, and may also be fined up to 1,000 yuan. Rule 5: Cotton handled by spinning mills, packing plants, or cotton firms must have the name of the firm clearly marked on the outside of the bale for easy investigation. Rule 6: Spinning mills, packing plants, or cotton firms that purchase wet cotton exceeding the maximum water content shall have their buying and selling and use suspended, and may also be fined up to 2,000 yuan. Rule 7: If a spinning mill purchases cotton with water content exceeding the standard but not exceeding the maximum limit, the price shall be deducted proportionally according to the water content. If the water content is below the standard, compensation shall be paid proportionally. Rule 8: If the cotton sold for future or spot delivery contains more cotton seeds or other impurities than the standard cotton agreed upon by both parties or the publicly agreed-upon standard cotton by more than 0.5%, the buying and selling and use shall be suspended, and a fine of up to 2,000 yuan shall be imposed. Rule 9: If the cotton sold for future or spot delivery contains more cotton seeds or other impurities than the standard cotton agreed upon by both parties or the publicly agreed-upon standard cotton by more than 0.5%, the percentage shall be deducted by double the amount. Rule 10: If fine cotton is mixed with coarse cotton, the selling price shall be calculated based on the price of coarse cotton. Rule 11: Cotton must be inspected and certified by a legal inspection agency before it can be imported. Rule 12: The Cotton Control Committee and various commodity inspection bureaus have the right to send personnel to cotton firms and factories for verification. Rule 13: If inspection personnel collude and engage in fraudulent practices, deliberately create difficulties, or nitpick when inspecting cotton, they shall be held criminally liable and shall also be liable for compensation if they harm the interests of the business operator as a result. Rule 14: The date of implementation of these rules shall be determined by order.

Municipal Federation Submits Petition to Abolish Electric Shock Torture to Uphold Legal Authority and Protect People's Lives

The First Special District Citizens' Federation submitted a petition to the Ministry of Judicial Administration yesterday, stating: "The petition concerns the abusive use of electric shock torture by the police, which cripples and kills people. We respectfully request that the Ministry investigate and address this issue strictly to uphold legal authority and protect people's lives. Torture has long been abolished in our country. However, the police in the Shanghai Concession have resumed this practice and even intensified it. Regardless of the case, any defendant who is arrested is subjected to electric shock torture to force a confession, which is then used as evidence of the defendant's own admission. Judges, without conducting proper investigations, are deceived by this practice and attach the confession to the case file as the basis for their verdict. Later, if the defendant wishes to argue their innocence, the questioners are already biased, making it difficult to overturn the verdict. The police's plan is thus successful, and the use of electric shock torture becomes widespread. The police's authority is limited to assisting the court in making arrests. After the arrest, they should be sent to the court for legal proceedings and have no need to force a confession. What is the police's intention in using this cruel electric shock torture? This is something that the association is not in a position to know. However, since the police began using electric shock torture to force confessions, countless innocent people have been framed. Recent cases such as those of Cai Yangqi and Chen Afu provide clear evidence to support this claim. Since the establishment of the Special District Court, much of the lost legal authority has been recovered. If this inhuman electric shock torture is not stopped, not only will people's lives be in danger, but legal authority will also be lost. For the sake of the country's legal authority and the people's lives, the association cannot remain silent. In addition to submitting separate reports to the Ministry of Foreign Affairs and the Municipal Government requesting them to lodge protests, we have also prepared a document to submit to the Ministry, respectfully requesting that you investigate and instruct the court to pay strict attention to this issue to uphold legal authority and protect people's lives. We are deeply grateful." Public Bus Hits Rickshaw, Two Children Injured and Killed: Russian Child Testifies Truck Was on the Wrong Route, Public Bus Could Not Avoid the Accident

Guangdong woman Cao Chen, along with her son Yonghong, age seven, and daughter Ai Kuan, age four, were riding in two rickshaws on Qu Ning Road and Zhapu Road, heading east to west, at around 7:00 AM the day before yesterday. At the same time, truck No. 16442, driven by Yang Kaimu, was also speeding west. However, the truck should have been traveling on the south side of the road, but it was traveling on the north side. At that time, public bus No. 15133, driven by Wu Jintang, was coming from the west. The two vehicles were about to collide, so Wu immediately turned the bus to the south side in an attempt to avoid the collision. However, the brakes failed, and the bus hit the two rickshaws one after another. Cao Chen and her two children were thrown from the rickshaws and were severely injured by the bus. The police arrived and recorded the numbers of the two vehicles and telephoned the Hongkou police station, ordering an ambulance to rush Ms. Cao and her three children to the Shanghai Sanatorium for treatment. However, the two children died due to their severe injuries. The police ordered detectives to investigate and took the two drivers back to the police station for detention. The bodies of the two children were sent to the Feilun Road morgue for examination. Yesterday morning, the police sent the two drivers to the Third Criminal Court of the First Special District District Court for public prosecution. Judge Xiao briefly interrogated them and adjourned the hearing. At around 10:00 AM, the prosecutor's office dispatched prosecutor Guo Wei, along with forensic doctors Wei and Zhang, and clerk Wang Zuyi, to the morgue for examination. After examining the bodies, they took testimony from a witness, Yiqin Bolang (transliteration), age twelve, a Russian resident of Park Lane and a student, who stated, "I happened to be passing by the area that day and saw the truck was on the wrong route. The public bus, fearing a collision, turned to the south and hit the two rickshaws. The truck was traveling very fast, and the public bus was traveling at a normal speed. I did not hear any horns from either vehicle. The truck did not stop after the accident." The father of the deceased, Cao Ziran, age thirty-six, a resident of No. 46 Dongbaoxing Road, Zhabei, and an employee at an oil factory, stated that the deceased were his children and that he was unaware of the accident at the time. He demanded compensation for all losses. Mr. Guo then questioned the two drivers and ruled that the boy, Cao Chenghong, and the girl, Cao Ai Kuan, had died from head and abdominal injuries caused by public bus No. 15133. Since truck driver Yang Kaimu and public bus driver Wu Jintang had already been publicly prosecuted by the police, they should be sent to the court for review. The bodies of the two children were handed over to their father, Cao Ziran, with a guarantee, to be taken back for coffin preparation.

Two Pirate Ships Rob Rice, Open Fire, and Kill a Crew Member; Small Boat Carrying Rice Encounters Robbers, Four Crew Members One Dead, Two Injured

Boatman Wang Botao has been purchasing rice in the interior and transporting it to Shanghai for sale. Recently, the price of rice in Shanghai has been rising, and he has made considerable profits from transporting rice from the interior three times in a row. The day before yesterday, he purchased more than 180 shi of rice from rural households in Wujiang and immediately set sail for Shanghai to sell it. Wang instructed his crew to travel day and night to reach Shanghai as soon as possible. Wang first took a train from Suzhou to Shanghai to contact merchants and negotiate sales. On the day before yesterday, Wang's boat was being sailed by his crew to a river near Dagang. The river's water level was low due to the prolonged drought, and the boat was grounded and unable to move. Seeing that the boat was grounded, the crew planned to wait for high tide to set sail. To their surprise, even when the tide rose in the afternoon, the boat was still unable to move. Since the boat's draft was very deep, the crew was about to hire a boat to transfer half of the rice to lighten the load and allow the boat to move when two small boats suddenly arrived in the evening. The crew, seeing that they looked like local boats, did not suspect anything and immediately asked the two small boats to carry the rice, agreeing to transport it to the Mao River. The two small boats agreed. Wang's crew transferred more than 80 shi of rice from the boat to the two small boats. After the transfer, the boat was lighter and able to move. The two small boats sailed ahead, and Wang's boat followed behind. Unexpectedly, when they reached the Mao River, the two small boats quickly raised their sails and sped away. Wang's crew ordered them to stop, but they ignored the order and continued to sail away. Wang's crew raised their sails to chase them and were about to catch up when the two small boats fired five or six shots at Wang's boat, killing one crew member and injuring two others. The boat was also hit by the shots. Of the four crew members on Wang's boat, only one was uninjured. At this point, they dared not chase any further and had to stop. The two pirate ships fled west. The crew reported the incident to the anti-smuggling patrol boat, which immediately gave chase. Yesterday, the crew arrived in Shanghai and reported the incident to the boat owner, Wang. Upon receiving the report, Wang immediately went to Gaoqiao and informed the family of the crew member who had been killed. They went to the boat together to prepare the body for transport back for burial. It is reported that the loss is estimated to be around 1,000 yuan.

Local Fruit Merchants Actively Develop Fruit Trade Organize Trade Companies and Economic Control Association for Pears and Hawthorns Standardize Tianjin Chestnut Prices and Organize Public Sales Market

China is located in the temperate zone with a warm climate, making it ideal for growing fruits. The Guangju oranges and Tianjin chestnuts produced here have long been famous at home and abroad. However, due to improper management, they have not been fully developed. Local fruit merchants are aware of this and are actively seeking ways to improve the situation. Recently, they have advocated for the public sale of Tianjin chestnuts, the organization of an economic control association for pears and hawthorns, and the establishment of trade companies to achieve the goal of development. Details are as follows:

Public Sale of Tianjin Chestnuts Has Become a Reality: Tianjin Liangxiang's chestnuts are fragrant, tender, and delicious, and are widely sold. The annual sales volume in this city has been in the tens of millions of dan or more. Since the profits are considerable, various merchants have engaged in fierce competition, causing the prices to fluctuate greatly, which has seriously harmed the market. Therefore, the local Fruit and Produce Trade Association has organized a public sales market for Tianjin chestnuts to set a precedent for standardized prices. Various organizational strategies have been formulated. The market is located at No. 16 Pu Iron Anchor Lane. The prices are determined by the fruit firms of Huitai, Yuankang, and Liang Dongsheng. The business hours are set from 6:00 AM to 5:00 PM daily.

Actively Organize Trade Companies: This city is located in a strategic location with people from home and abroad gathered here. The consumption of fruits is the highest in the country, and trade is frequent. Although there were previously one or two import merchants managing these matters, they lacked competition and experience, resulting in a lack of progress. Furthermore, the matters entrusted by fruit merchants often failed due to various barriers. Therefore, it was decided to organize a trade company named Youhua, specializing in the import and export of fruits. It has already been established and is of great scale.

Establish Economic Control Committee for Pears and Hawthorns: According to the person in charge of the Fruit and Produce Trade Association, the pears and hawthorns needed in this city are mostly produced in Tianjin Teng County and Nanjing, with those produced in Xihe, Yuhe, and Botou being particularly good. Currently, the fruit industry has organized an economic control association for pears and hawthorns to control the trade of pears and hawthorns. There are currently twenty-one merchants who have joined, and recently two more companies, Xie Feng and Tai Feng, have joined, making the organization very tight-knit.

Notice to Members Requiring Payment of Security Deposits: The local Fruit and Produce Trade Association issued a notice yesterday stating that the association's fourth member meeting had resolved to organize an economic control association for pears and hawthorns and to handle matters in accordance with the draft plan presented by the county. The organization has been completed and a meeting was convened with related businesses on June 22. At the meeting, it was decided that Bao Cheng, Ling Feng, Dong Shenglong, Yi Yuande, Yuankang, Yongda, Shengda, Xie Yuan, Huitai, Xie Mao, and Wufeng would be Type A members and would be required to pay a security deposit of 500 yuan. Long Mao, He Kang, Yonghe, Zhang Hengmao, Dasheng, Tong Xiangmao, Qianji, Yongfeng, Xie Shengyuan, and Yuanfeng would be Type B members and would be required to pay a security deposit of 300 yuan with a monthly interest rate of 7%, and to sign a membership contract by the deadline. All security deposits must be paid in full by July 10. The sales volume and amount of Tianjin Botou Teng County Nanjing Jinan pears and hawthorns (excluding Qingdao and Yantai) sold in the last three years, from July 20 to June 23, must be submitted to the association for review by July 10, along with the records for the past three years, to compile the total amount and determine the standard ratio. All members are hereby notified to comply with this notice. Please do not delay the submission of the required information. This notice is hereby issued.

Police Officer Arbitrarily Releases Detained Suspect; Paramour Flees and Does Not Return; Qin Guo Shi Secretly Flees from Her Husband; Gu Jin Song is Freed; Police Officer Zhu Yuan Ji Takes Custody

Qin Zhao Yu, from Gao You, resides at No. 204, Yue Zhou Road, Yang Shu Pu. In the 19th year of the Republic of China, he married Guo Shi, a woman from the same village. They had a son who is now only three years old, and their relationship was quite good. However, although Guo Shi came from a humble background, she was not unattractive. As a result, many lecherous men pursued her. Guo Shi was also known for her promiscuity, seemingly open to anyone being her husband. Her scandalous reputation spread far and wide. Now, she became intimate with a man named Gu Jin Song and suddenly, on the 17th day of the lunar May, she secretly fled from her husband without a trace. Her mother asked a neighbor, Liu Qing Zhi, to find her. Liu, in turn, entrusted Ye A Kun and Jing Yuan Gui to search in all directions. They learned that Guo Shi and Gu Jin Song had rented a house in the Zhong Xing Road area, and they reported this to Qin Zhao Yu. The day before yesterday, Qin went to the address and found Gu, but Guo Shi had already escaped. Gu was taken to the fifth district police station on Heng Bang Road and temporarily detained. Shortly afterward, Liu Qing Zhi, accompanied by Gu Jin Song's aunt, Gu Zheng Shi, went to the police station to visit. Liu discussed with the guard, police officer Zhu Yuan Ji, to swap Gu Zheng Shi for Gu Jin Song, allowing him to go out and find Qin Guo Shi. Unexpectedly, Gu Jin Song left and did not return. The next day, when Qin Zhao Yu went to the police station to request the arrest of Qin Guo Shi, he discovered that the captured Gu Jin Song had been secretly released. Based on this information, he reported to the Fifth District Police Bureau to detain Liu Qing Zhi, Gu Zheng Shi, and the police officer Zhu Yuan Ji, who had arbitrarily released the suspect. During interrogation, Zhu Yuan Ji confessed that Gu Jin Song, who was in custody, was guaranteed by the familiar Liu Qing Zhi, who brought Gu's aunt, Gu Zheng Shi, to swap places, so that Gu could find and return Qin Guo Shi. Liu Qing Zhi claimed that he had served in the police force before the January 28th Incident, which is why he knew Zhu, but denied acting as a guarantor. Yesterday morning, upon instruction, the plaintiff Qin Zhao Yu, witnesses Ye A Kun and Jing Yuan Gui, and the defendants Zhu Yuan Ji, Liu Qing Zhi, and Gu Zheng Shi were all transferred to the local court for further investigation.

Drought Causes Rivers to Run Shallow; Vegetable and Melon Prices Rise

This summer has been plagued by a severe drought. Despite prayers for rain from various charitable organizations, no rain has fallen. Although there were clouds the day before yesterday, the sun quickly reappeared, making the heat unbearable. Recently, farmers have been irrigating their fields day and night, causing rivers to gradually dry up. Watermelons and other melons lack natural rain irrigation, so the water quality is also inferior to previous years. Ships find it difficult to navigate, and the number of tugboats operated by shipping companies has decreased, leading to a gradual reduction in supply. According to the local Produce Trade Association, if it does not rain in the next week, the supply of various vegetables in the city will inevitably decrease, and market prices will rise. Melon prices are already one-third higher than last week. If it does not rain in the next week, shallow rivers will prevent ships from passing, reducing the number of vessels and cutting off supplies. The demand for vegetables and melons in the city will inevitably exceed supply.

Shanghai Municipal Council to Issue Rickshaw Licenses Based on Ownership Certificates

The Shanghai Municipal Council has decided that, starting in August, applications for public rickshaw (yellow rickshaw) licenses (also known as permits) will only be granted to those who hold an ownership certificate issued by the Rickshaw Affairs Committee. The ownership certificates have already been scheduled for issuance in June and July, and rickshaw owners are requested to apply on the designated dates. As of now, applications for approximately 700 certificates have been received. However, the actual number of applications received from rickshaw owners is less than this number. As a result, some public rickshaw licenses may be suspended or issued to other rickshaw owners who are willing to fully comply with the Council's regulations.

Because some existing rickshaw owners refuse to apply for certificates, there may be some changes in the rickshaw business, and there may be a temporary shortage of vehicles. However, the Council is determined to implement its measures and prevent all illegal or intimidating actions. Due to the refusal of rickshaw owners to apply for certificates, some rickshaw pullers may suffer unemployment. Therefore, the Rickshaw Affairs Committee has decided that if the number of applications from existing rickshaw owners is insufficient, it will accept applications from new rickshaw owners or allow existing rickshaw owners who are willing to comply with the Council's regulations to request an expansion of their fleet. These requests must be submitted between July 25th and 29th, either by mail or special delivery, to Office 512 in the Shanghai Municipal Council General Office, addressed to the Rickshaw Affairs Committee. A receipt will be issued. The application must include the name (or names in the case of a partnership), address, guarantor, and the number of vehicles the applicant wishes to operate. All applicants must comply with the Council's newly established regulations for public rickshaw licenses. The Council will give priority to issuing licenses to those who are willing to cooperate in establishing a rickshaw pullers' mutual aid society.

Rickshaw Guild Issues Declaration; Refutes the Rickshaw Committee's Measures Point by Point

According to the Xin Sheng News Agency, the Shanghai Rickshaw Trade Special District Office, dissatisfied with the Shanghai Municipal Council's Rickshaw Committee's nitpicking, resolved in a special committee meeting to invite people from all walks of life at a set time. Yesterday, it issued a declaration stating: "We, the rickshaw merchants, have had a long and distinguished history of several decades since the start of our business. We have always been under the direct jurisdiction of the Shanghai Municipal Council's Rickshaw Affairs Office. Rickshaw owners are diligent and thrifty, and rickshaw pullers work day and night. As a result, the business has developed day by day, and everyone has lived in peace. Who knew that this would stir the desire for wealth in one or two Westerners, coupled with the encouragement of unscrupulous Chinese, and the Rickshaw Affairs Committee came into being. The Committee, under the guise of saving rickshaw pullers and improving rickshaw affairs, has been promoting itself everywhere as a savior for rickshaw pullers, but the result is equal to zero, only fulfilling the Committee members' massive monthly salaries of thousands of gold coins. What is most surprising is that the measures and plans formulated by the Committee are completely incompatible with the customs of the rickshaw industry, with nothing right about them. It is truly like building a car behind closed doors, never getting on the right track. Now, we will select the main points from the Committee's sixteen measures, which it considers successful, for comment (so that it can be known that the Committee is stealing the superficiality of social theories, which is absolutely not conducive to practical application). For example, in the Committee's first, second, and third articles, it is stated that the original rickshaws of each rickshaw owner will be gradually reduced year by year and handed over to another new rickshaw company for operation. May we ask, is this kind of action applicable in any country? Even before or after the Soviet Union's Five-Year Plan, has there ever been such administrative action? It must be known that even a single rickshaw is a life and property, and it must not be unconditionally taken back or given to another operator at will. Fortunately, the authorities deeply understand that it is impractical and have generally reserved and shelved it. The phrase 'genuine rickshaw owner' in the fifth article on registration is even more nitpicking. It must be known that a rickshaw owner is always a rickshaw owner, there is no such thing as genuine or fake. The former system of paying donations on behalf of others was stipulated by the Shanghai Municipal Council, requiring at least twenty rickshaws to establish a guarantee, and requiring a reliable shop guarantee or additional payment of a deposit. It was absolutely impossible for rickshaw owners with a small number of rickshaws to directly report the donation. They could only combine several rickshaw owners with a small number of rickshaws to form an integer and report the donation to the Shanghai Municipal Council on their behalf. In fact, it only facilitated the Shanghai Municipal Council's handling procedures. For decades, responsibilities have been distinguished and have not been disrupted. It can be seen that the system of paying donations on behalf of others, although not satisfactory to the newly established Rickshaw Affairs Committee, has also been meritorious. The sixth article on registering rickshaw pullers and improving rickshaws is the responsibility of the Rickshaw Affairs Office and is absolutely not a way to improve the lives of rickshaw pullers. How can it be mentioned together? The Committee's view is so naive and pathetic. The eighth article, under the guise of registering rickshaw pullers, actually requires rickshaw pullers to pay a registration fee, which is extremely despicable. At a time when trams and cars are competing for passengers, the ninth article actually wants to increase rickshaw fares. Its intention is vicious, actually driving fish into the deep sea and reducing the business of rickshaw pullers. The ninth and tenth articles are even more obvious acts of sabotage. If new rickshaws are replaced, they should be gradually replaced from old and worn rickshaws. It is absolutely impossible to stamp a new rickshaw shell today and change the new rickshaw style tomorrow. These significant losses are all borne by the rickshaw owners, which is of no benefit to the country or the people. The fifteenth article severely cracks down on illegal rickshaws, benefiting public rickshaw pullers. Who knew that there would be no action for several months? It is well known that illegal rickshaws are a personal scourge to public rickshaw pullers. Thirty percent of the floating capital under transportation goes to illegal rickshaws. If the authorities are willing to do their duty, they should have made an expression long ago. It is easy and pleasant, why not do it? It can rectify the rickshaw regulations and increase the income of public rickshaw pullers. The Committee makes empty promises of relief and liberation, only looking for flaws in form and color. In the end, it sacrifices the property of rickshaw merchants, reduces much prosperity in the market, and fulfills the titles of several sociologists. Now the Shanghai Municipal Council does not remember the past achievements of the rickshaw merchants and is alarmed by the alarmist talk of one or two people. It has specially formed a redundant organization with high positions and high salaries, buying peace and quiet. Originally, the Committee members are all sociologists who have always been well-fed and well-housed, sitting high and grand. They must not have dreamed of the lives of rickshaw pullers and the work of the lower class, let alone experienced it in person. They only make contradictory claims based on empty ideals, which are impractical and unreasonable. For half a year, the rickshaw pullers have not received blessings, and the rickshaw merchants have suffered endlessly. We had no choice but to convene a general meeting of all rickshaw owners on June 18th, together with the Council, and unanimously decided to organize a special committee of the Shanghai Rickshaw Trade Association Special District Office, so as to concentrate our efforts and carry out negotiations. All illegal points and contradictory claims of the Committee will be corrected. After the Committee realizes and corrects, we will accept them. Finally, we also intend to appeal to all sectors for assistance, make a practical expression of strength, awaken public opinion, and make a fair criticism. Our Association represents all rickshaw owners in their unanimous struggle, fighting for their last lives. At present, the summer season has arrived. Regarding the temporary relief, our Association, based on the spirit of mutual assistance, attaches importance to actual implementation. In addition to depositing the existing 50,000 gold coins with the custody committee for safekeeping, we still ask the rickshaw owners' general meeting and the Council to continue to provide medical care, medicine, coffins, and tea to seek the happiness of rickshaw pullers. We hereby declare this, hoping for your public attention."

The Zhabei Water and Electricity Company has always paid attention to the quality of drinking water. It is reported that the factory has four new American-style green gas sterilization machines, which have excellent sterilization effects. Gao Qiao Shi Abuses Adopted Daughter; Burns Face with Fire; Landlady Voices Outrage

Gao Qiao Shi, a woman from Ningbo, 38 years old, lives at No. 21, You Zhi Nong Lane, outside the Small South Gate. In 1931, due to a lack of children, she purchased a girl in Wuxi and brought her home, naming her Jin Mei, and raising her to this day, now six years old. However, she is known for her shrewish nature, so Jin Mei is often whipped and even starved if she displeases her. Her neighbors also express outrage. Yesterday afternoon around 4:00 PM, Jin Mei accidentally angered her over a trivial matter, and Gao Qiao Shi actually placed a roll of newspaper on the ground, set it on fire, and then tied the girl's hands with hemp rope. She forcefully pressed the girl's head down, causing her face to be scorched by the fire. At that time, Jin Mei was unable to resist due to her young age and weakness. Her face was burned by the fire, blistering and festering, and bleeding profusely. The landlady, Hou Jiang Shi, heard the screams and rushed over. Unable to bear the sight, she secretly slipped out and summoned the watchman Shi Cheng Qi of the 19th station. Shi Cheng Qi arrested Gao Qiao Shi and took her and Jin Mei to the First Precinct, First Station. After questioning by Chief Yi, he found that the girl was covered in scars and wounds. He deemed Gao Qiao Shi's abuse of her adopted daughter inhumane and ordered a formal report to be submitted to the Municipal Public Security Bureau for strict investigation and punishment.

One Year Since the Collision of the "Tunan"; The Japanese Verdict is Rebutted Again; The Japanese Demand Compensation; Our Side Rebuts Again and Lodges a Stern Protest

It has been one year since the merchant ship "Tunan" was sunk by the Japanese ship "Changchun Maru" in the Shandong sea area last year. After the "Tunan" was sunk, our side advocated organizing an arbitration tribunal in Shanghai, but the Dalian Steamship Company refused and even sent a letter to the China Merchants Bureau demanding more than 70,000 yuan for various losses of the "Changchun Maru." If not paid, they threatened to detain our ships. Upon receiving this news, the China Merchants Bureau investigated the total losses of the "Tunan," including the value of the sunken passengers and goods, and submitted a detailed list to the Ministry of Foreign Affairs, formally requesting negotiations with the Japanese Ministry of Foreign Affairs to order the Dalian Steamship Company to promptly compensate for the losses. Four months later, the Dalian Steamship Company finally replied, stating that the case had been judged by the Dalian Kwantung Office Maritime Court, holding the Chinese ship responsible and stating that the "Changchun Maru" bore no responsibility. The judgment was made on September 12th of last year by Okamoto Makoto, Chairman of the Kwantung Office Ship Disciplinary Committee, as well as Committee Members Eara Mikiki, Kwan Sai Shiroya and others, for the owner of the "Changchun Maru," Kashiwagi Hachiro, stating that the "Changchun Maru" was sailing without error and would not be subject to disciplinary action. The judgment was based purely on the statements of Japanese crew members from the "Tongji Maru," "Toka Maru," and "Azuma Maru," as well as the second mate Konno and the second engineer Matsuyama of the "Changchun Maru." The reports of the crew members of our country's "Tunan" were completely ignored, resulting in a one-sided judgment that did not conform to the facts. It is reported that the China Merchants Bureau will carefully rebut the judgment document based on the facts and submit it to the central government again, requesting a stern protest to achieve the purpose of compensation, clarify right and wrong, and promote justice.

Japanese Residents in Shanghai; Attach Importance to the Taiwan Consular Conference

According to the Central News Agency, the Japanese Consulate in this port revealed that the Japanese will hold a South China Japanese Consular Conference in Taiwan tomorrow (the 16th). The meeting will be held at the Governor-General's Office in Taipei. Japanese consuls from Xiamen, Fuzhou, Shantou, Shamian, and Hong Kong, as well as Counselor Yamada representing Minister Arima, Sato, the First Section Chief of the Asia Bureau of the Ministry of Foreign Affairs, and Takahashi, representing the Ministry of Colonial Affairs, have all gone to participate. This conference is very important and will be presided over by the Governor-General of Taiwan. The conference will last for three days, and the agenda will include: (1) Matters of liaison between the South China consuls and the Governor-General's Office of Taiwan; (2) Issues of promoting trade between Taiwan and the ports on the opposite shore; (3) Issues of controlling the migration of Taiwanese people to South China; (4) Issues of increasing Taiwan and South China Sea aquatic products. Japanese residents in this port attach great importance to this South China Consular Conference.

County Government Orders the Combination of District Chiefs

Shanghai County is divided into six autonomous districts. Now, the county government, in accordance with the provincial order, has merged the Third and Sixth Districts into one, still named the Third District Office, located in Beiqiao Town. Mr. Pan Zhongjia, the county magistrate, has appointed Wang Chengyao to take over the position of District Chief. The former District Chief, Sun Shiben, has been appointed as an accountant at the County Property Office. Wang, the new district chief, is from Maqiao in this county and has served as the head of the Rural Administration Bureau and the head of the Sixth District. The Third and Sixth Districts have been combined, and the Maqiao Sixth District Office will be abolished immediately. The chiefs and deputies of the merged townships have also been selected and appointed by the county. Therefore, the county government will report the situation of the county's districts and townships to the provincial government for record.

Resolutions

After the chairman's report, the discussion began. Regarding the negotiation of the detention of coal ships by the inspection station:

Ministry of Communications to Crack Down on Abuse of Public Telegrams

The Ministry of Communications recently issued a special order to the Shanghai Radio Administration Bureau regarding the crackdown on the abuse of public telegrams. The order stated that public telegrams were originally established for urgent official business, and under no circumstances should they be sent arbitrarily for non-urgent official business. Repeated orders had been issued to comply with this. In order to effectively crack down on the abuse of public telegrams, the bureau was ordered to conduct spot checks on the underlying telegrams of the bureaus under its jurisdiction at any time, strictly assess them in accordance with the Ministry of Communications' regulations for the issuance of public telegrams by telecommunications agencies, and submit a list to the ministry for future reference on a monthly basis, including the bureau that issued the telegram, the date of the public telegram, and the number. If there are public telegrams that are not sent in accordance with the public telegram rules, they should be copied and submitted to the ministry for punishment.

Reading and Answering Questions

Scientific Spiritualism and Ghosts and Gods丨Reply to Mr. Li Jiasheng丨

[Scientific Spiritualism Chart] was popular for a month or two, but now this craze is gradually cooling down. Presumably, many people have been fooled and realized that it is a deceptive thing. However, its impact on the general public is still quite significant. Many people are still half-believing and half-doubting, such as Mr. Li Jiasheng and others who have written to inquire about this matter. He said that he had personally tested this spiritualism and that everything answered through this spiritualism regarding past events was accurate. He felt that this was truly [mysterious] and [profound], and it could not be understood without explaining it through ghosts and gods.

The principle of spiritualism has been discussed in various newspaper supplements and magazines before, and it seems that we do not need to spend much effort on it now. However, now that people are still asking about this matter, it can be known that many people are still hoping for an answer. At least, we still need to provide a more accessible and clearer explanation so that the general public can understand the true nature of this ghost and not be deceived by it.

Let's first talk about the principle of spiritualism. Although spiritualism seems mysterious to the general public, it is a very ordinary and simple thing when explained by psychology. In a word: spiritualism is nothing more than a kind of [unconscious behavior]. Unconscious behavior is something that people do unconsciously. Many of our behaviors are unintentional and unconscious. This kind of unconscious behavior is mostly due to habit. For example, a person who closes the windows every day before going out will often unconsciously go to close the windows naturally after a long time. Also, when we walk on the road, we can just think about other things, but our feet can walk naturally, turning when encountering a turn, and avoiding when encountering an obstacle, unconsciously walking a long distance [without even realizing it]. When one is excessively concerned and attentive to a certain thing, unconscious behavior will also occur. For example, the phenomenon of sleepwalking, where one can get up in the middle of the night and do things that were not finished during the day, is because they were very concerned about this matter during the day. The secret of hypnosis lies in finding a way to make the subject use their own commands to cause the subject's unconscious actions. As for the principle of spiritualism, it also utilizes unconscious actions during concentrated attention. The movement of the saucer in the center of the spiritualism chart is not actually caused by ghosts touching it, but because the person holding the planchette's fingers have been suspended under the saucer for half an hour, and on the one hand, their arm has become sore and numb and naturally trembling, thus pushing the saucer. On the other hand, because their attention has been focused on the spiritualism chart, their own arm is pushing the saucer, but they do not know it, and instead think that the saucer is moving by itself. As for the subsequent summoning of ghosts and conversations, and inquiries about things, it is still the result of unconscious actions. Mr. Li said that everything asked about past events was accurate because everything in the past was already a foregone conclusion in the minds of Mr. Li and his peers, and the answers were all made by Mr. Li and his peers themselves, but Mr. Li and his peers were not aware of it. Moreover, spiritualism can only accurately tell us about past events. For future events, the answers of spiritualism are completely unreliable. A pregnant woman asked whether she would give birth to a boy or a girl, and the spiritualism answered that she would give birth to a boy, but in reality, she later gave birth to a girl. This is because the woman's hope for a boy was unintentionally expressed in the spiritualism, and it was definitely not a ghost deceiving her! In addition, such as buying aviation lottery tickets and flower clubs, some people have also asked about the numbers, but no one has ever succeeded! The deceptiveness of the spiritualism chart can be understood very clearly here.

Ghosts and gods do not exist. People with scientific common sense do not need to doubt this matter anymore. Feuerbach said, [God is created by man.] The Chinese proverb also says: [Suspicion breeds ghosts.] Ghosts and gods are tools used by a portion of the privileged class in society to deceive the public. When the public is deceived, they believe that their fate is controlled by ghosts and gods, and do not know that the root of their suffering lies in society, and cannot face and observe society. The public should no longer be fooled by blind faith, should no longer be content with the dictates of fate, and should observe their surroundings with a scientific eye to find their true way out.

In the current era of economic panic, most people are suffering from a lack of livelihood. The only way to solve the livelihood of the masses is to see this society clearly and deal with everything with a positive attitude. However, some people cannot recognize this point. They covet ease and seek luck, so aviation lottery tickets, flower clubs, etc., have become their best way to solve their livelihood. Indeed, one win is tens of thousands of yuan, how can it not be good? But what about reliability! It is simply like looking for a needle in a haystack, so many people are still suffering from a lack of certainty. The scientific spiritualism chart has seized on this point and has come forward in big strides, writing guarantees to people, saying that it can definitely know the winning numbers in advance. People eager to win, therefore, rush to buy spiritualism charts and rush to buy aviation tickets, but in the end, who has really won the prize? We have never seen it.

People who hope for luck are the most pitiful. They are deceived and trampled on without knowing it. If we want to avoid repeating the same mistakes, we must earnestly recognize the world and recognize society through scientific research. At the same time, we must see clearly that the so-called scientific spiritualism chart is just a superstitious tool that deceives people under the guise of science.

Spring and Autumn Children's Weekly

Ideals and Will

— Zhang Muliang

Humans have various ideals, and then they have various new inventions and new constructions, so they can create today's bright and splendid world. If humans did not have ideals, where would there be any new inventions or new constructions?

Although we have very grand ideals, if we are not willing to do them practically, the result will only be empty dreams, fantasies, and reveries!

Children! Do you have ideals? Do you want your ideals to come true? If you want your ideals to come true, you should strengthen your will and move forward on the path of your ideals, then you can realize your ideals.

Children! Do you remember? In the country of Sparta, a young man said to his mother: [My sword:] [If the sword is too short, I can make it longer myself.] In fact, it doesn't seem strange, but from a young age, he cultivated the spirit of creation and a strong will, which is what we should know.

Dear children! If you have the spirit of creation and a strong will, how can your ideals not become a reality?

Zeng Wenzheng Achieved Success by Practicing a New Life

— Da Zhai

Zeng Wenzheng's morality, meritorious deeds, calligraphy, and writing are all known to be very good. Inquiring into why he had such great achievements, it is indeed derived from practicing a new life.

When Zeng Wenzheng was young, he started reading at the age of five, and by the age of nine, he had finished reading the Five Classics thoroughly. At that time, there were no elementary school textbooks, but he was willing to follow the methods of teaching people mentioned in the Five Classics. He studied the Book of Zhou Rites and the Book of Rites at the age of fifteen, so he paid great attention to etiquette. It can be seen that he had already formed the habit of learning from the Five Classics in his childhood.

How can it be seen that he was practicing a new life! Isn't it like an association? There is evidence, called being true to one's name.

Zeng Wenzheng's name was Guofan. The two characters Guofan are taken from the meaning of [protecting the country and building a fence], which means that he was determined to do something for the country in the future. At the age of twenty-one, he changed his nickname to Disheng. He himself said: The character "di" means to wash away the pollution of the old dyeing, and the character "sheng" is taken from Yuan Liaofan of the Ming Dynasty, who said, [All the past, like yesterday's death, all the future, like today's birth.] We see that his explanation of the meaning of Disheng is exactly in line with the three characters of the current new life, but at that time, there was no new vocabulary for this new knowledge.

It is inevitable that people will make mistakes. If you realize that you are doing something wrong, you should immediately change it. It's like very dirty things, which can only be renewed by scrubbing hard: It's like coming back to life after death, no longer following the old path of death, and moving forward on the bright road: The so-called [correct them if you have them, and encourage yourself if you don't,] practicing a new life like this will naturally lead to the achievement of virtue and career.

Children, savor the two characters Disheng, reflect on your clothing, food, housing, and transportation at all times, set a good example, practice a new life, and prepare to be a barrier to the country and save the country from danger.

Hands and Legs

— Liu Yaotong

We all have two hands:

Don't hide them in your sleeves,

Do your own things yourself,

Don't rely on parents and friends.

Arms as thick as tree trunks,

Fists as big as dippers,

Swordsmanship and martial arts are well-trained,

Grow up to avenge the country in the future.

X X X

Don't always put them on the table,

Practice running and high jumping more,

Muscles trained like iron blocks.

Recognize your goals and walk quickly,

Don't be afraid of obstacles on the road.

You should always be ahead,

Don't come back until you reach your goal.

How to Pay Attention to Summer Hygiene

— Rizhao

Children, summer is the season when flies and mosquitoes are rampant. If we are not careful, we will get sick. Rather than taking that sour and bitter medicine after getting sick, it is better to be careful in advance. The following are the items that we must practice every day.

(1) Clothes: The best color for clothes is white, because white repels sunlight. And you should change your clothes at least once a day, and don't wear them when they are wet with sweat.

(2) Food: Don't eat too much oil, it is best to eat vegetarian food, but don't overeat. Do not eat overnight food. Do not eat cold drinks from street vendors. It is best to drink cold boiled water.

(3) Living: Windows should be opened often to allow air to circulate. Drains and other dirty places should be frequently sprayed with disinfectant. Do not sleep in the open at night.

(4) Bathing: In summer, take a bath at least once a day. It is advisable to wash with warm water, and after washing, you must wipe dry with a dry towel.

(5) Other: It is best to take a nap for a while in the afternoon, and take a walk in the evening. Wear a straw hat when going out, and do not go naked.

Simple Balloon

— Zijing

Haha! I often make this balloon to play with. The method is extremely easy, so it is named a simple balloon. Children, if you have time, you can make one in an open space to play with.

Supplies: Machine-made paper, bamboo sticks, thin iron wire, broken cotton, tung oil. Production method: Cut out several pieces of machine-made paper (Figure 1), which can be enlarged at will. After cutting, paste them with flour paste to prevent leaks (as in Figure 2). Use bamboo sticks to make a ring at the bottom (as in the size of the balloon opening), and glue it to the opening of the paper balloon: Then use iron wire to make a net (as in Figure 2), press it on the bamboo stick at the balloon opening: Then wrap broken cotton with tung oil, light it in the net, and hold it upright by two people. If it is slightly off, it will easily burn. After a while, the inside of the balloon is filled with black gas, and when you let go, it will gradually rise.

Methods of Protecting Brainpower

— Ling

Children: Your brainpower must be very clever, but some children may not be as good as you. Then clever children must always protect their cleverness well. I will tell you the methods of protecting brainpower to avoid the decline of brainpower.

Don't be angry often, because after getting angry, blood flowing into the brain is easy to damage the brain. It is best to always be peaceful.

You must wear a hat or umbrella when going out, because direct sunlight on the brain is also easy to damage the brain: Alcohol is even more likely to damage the brain, so you should never drink or smoke it in your life.

The above are all good ways to protect the brain. Children: You are still young now, and your brainpower is at its most sensitive period. Then often use these protection methods. When you reach adulthood, you will definitely have a scientific mind, and you can invent all kinds of beneficial tools to defeat the great enemy of China.

Why Can Fish Float and Swim

— Tiansheweng

Crucian carp, carp, perch, etc. swim back and forth in the water, swimming up and down, lively and free, very happy. For example, our little brothers, little sisters, children, parade in the park in teams. They are all breathing free air and enjoying free happiness. People and fish are generally happy.

But, I think: people's walking and running rely on two feet. What about fish: the caudal fin is the rudder, and the pectoral and pelvic fins are the oars: the oars are used for forward movement: the rudder is used to turn the direction: the principles of fish and boats being able to move in water are indeed the same. People in ancient times invented ships after seeing fish swimming. Modern airplanes were invented after seeing birds. Children! What else can we invent?

Fins are fish's traveling companions. Why can fish float and sink in water, sometimes up and sometimes down? Sometimes, the head floats on the surface of the water, and the tail sinks in the water. Sometimes, the tail floats on the surface of the water, and the head rushes to the bottom of the water. Floating up and down is extremely convenient. What is the reason for this?

Let's try to cut open the belly of a fish. In addition to the intestines and stomach, isn't there also a silvery-white cyst? This thing is called a "swim bladder," which is the fish's tool for floating up and down. The swim bladder is divided into two parts, front and back. Each part is a leathery, long, oval sphere, which stores air. When floating, the air in the swim bladder is full. The fish then floats to the center of the water. When the air is released from the swim bladder, the fish then sinks into the water. If you want the head to be up and the tail to be down, then the front part of the swim bladder is full of air, and the rear part is released. If you want the head to be down and the tail to be up, then the rear part of the swim bladder is full of air, and the front part is released. In this way, fish can lively and freely float up and down.

Even if we carry a large leather bag full of air, we won't sink to the bottom of the water, even if someone can't swim. It's the same principle.

Small Experience

Mildew and Moth Prevention

— Jianfen

Children: During the rainy season, I think your homes have a little bit of stored books: you'd better move the stored books out on a sunny day and put them in the sun to dry.

After drying, add a little [broken camphor] (sold in pharmacies) and夹it in the books. In this way: the stored books will not mold or moth in the mildew. The reason is: mold must grow in damp places, and mold cannot live in dry places: when you dry the books, the sunlight has already evaporated the moisture in the books, and the books are very dry: then you put in camphor, camphor can kill蛀bugs: so mold and蛀bugs cannot invade your books, so your books will be completely worry-free. However, you cannot rely on this once and for all. Because over time, dry objects will become damp due to the air climate: and camphor will also lose its effectiveness over a long period of time. So you must also check it often and pay attention to it.

(PS) Children: If your books have been found to be moldy or蛀by bugs: you can quickly do it according to the above method, don't hold on to a passive doctrine. Because [it's better to mend the fold after the sheep is lost] than [to lose it again and again].

Methods of Planting Flowers and Trees

— Xu Zongjie

Dear children! Do you like trees, flowers, and plants? If you like them, you might as well plant some more in your schoolyard or in the gaps in your home. When the trees grow up and the flowers bloom, things that you plant and grow yourself will make you extremely happy once you get results.

Some plants are grown from seeds, which is convenient, and I don't need to say much about it here. Some plants are propagated by cuttings of branches, which is not an easy task. I now have some small experiences to contribute to you. This is what I have verified, you might as well try it.

Cut off the branches of various trees in winter, excluding those that are too tender or too old, and plant them upside down in sandy soil mixed with fine soil: they should be exposed to sunlight, and it is best not to be pressed by frost and snow. When the vernal equinox arrives, plant the upside-down branches upright in the soil, and they will sprout and grow leaves.

It is best to divide and transplant roses and the like before the vernal equinox. Cut off the branches that are not too tender or too old, insert them into the whole sugarcane, and plant them in the soil together, watering them often, and they will not easily die.

When breaking off gardenia, do not simply插it in the soil. Insert it in a vase for供養, as long as the water in the vase does not dry up, it will naturally grow whiskers, and it will be easy to grow after being buried in the soil after the flowers wither.

Small Jokes

— Ku Xuesheng

(1) One Hundred Points

After dinner, I was walking in the playground with classmate Zhiming. He reported the results of today's monthly exam. He said: [I got one hundred points on today's exam.] People listened to his words, and then very happily asked him: [Which subject is it?] He quickly replied to me: [Common knowledge is fifty points, and Chinese is fifty points. Isn't it exactly one hundred points when added together]?

(2) Who is the most honest person in the world?

Brother asks: [Brother! Do you know who is the most honest person in the world?

Brother answers: [Brother! The person who sells stinky tofu on the street is the most honest.

Brother further asked: [How do you know he is the most honest person?]

Brother also answers: [Because his tofu is stinky, when he sells it, isn't he loudly shouting stinky tofu? This is irrefutable evidence of not cheating people, so I praise him as the most honest person in the world]!

Correspondence from Rural Little Friends

— Ziming

Dear Children:

The sun is blushing and walking down obliquely: At this time, there are three or two spiders at the corners of the eaves, pulling silk from their bellies, using their flexible eight legs, making a few circles, and a bagua-shaped net is張good, it stands in the middle with great prestige: like the commander of the Bagua Formation.

However, although the spider is an insect, it has great perseverance. If, when making a net, it encounters a howling wind. The delicate silk cannot withstand the wind and breaks. The spider ignores it: it only believes that [hard work] can overcome everything: so it breaks and does it again, breaks and does it again: finally, it still wins with hard work, and still张the Bagua net, and becomes the commander itself. However, when a heavy rain comes, it is always被打落花流水, and there is no place to stand. However, after the dark snow is pushed away, it is again

Operating and destroying the fortress of flying insects.

Why do spiders work so hard? Friends! They and we humans are also in [competition for survival]! They put down the Bagua Formation, and I don't know how many small insects that fly freely in the sky are happily trapped in the net and become the food of the commander.

It is right to kill many pests: but it still kills beneficial insects such as dragonflies as usual, knowing only that it is food for the belly, so the friendly and peaceful Chinese cannot be blamed for being bullied by the Japanese.

Birds and Fish in a Wooden Box

— Linghu Zhao

An empty wooden box weighs five pounds when suspended. If there are birds flying around inside, will the pointer still point to five pounds? Suppose this wooden box is filled with water and weighs fifteen pounds, and then a fish is put in, the water is still full, and the fish is swimming in the water, will the weight increase?

Children, you can understand by looking at the picture on the left. Although the bird does not stop in the box, when it flies, its two wings flap down, and the air pressure increases, so the weight on the scales also increases and does not stop at five pounds. Fish are a little different in water. Archimedes' theorem in physics tells us: [Water has buoyancy, and the weight of things in water is exactly equal to the weight of water displaced]. So the fish's wooden box is still fifteen pounds!
