Education News: Ministry of Education's Instructions on Key Points for Improvement in Schools Above the Specialty Level in Beiping (2)

National Beiping Normal University

The school's operation is still lacking in good results. The following are the points that should be improved:

(1) In terms of the school's equipment, the library and auditorium are not suitable for use, there are very few complete sets of scientific journals, and the contents of the chemistry department's medicine and instrument room are not yet sufficient. It has been found that the school has as many as 172 staff members and 228 school servants and guards, which is too many. They should be reduced as much as possible, and administrative expenses should be saved for the purpose of enriching equipment.

(2) The school has 135 teachers, only 37 of whom are full-time, and many of the full-time teachers are still employed part-time outside the school. The school's important staff members also hold positions such as president and department head in other schools, which is inappropriate and should be corrected. Full-time teachers should be hired as much as possible, and strict measures should be formulated to restrict part-time teaching outside the school. Presidents, department heads, and other important responsible personnel should absolutely not hold part-time positions outside the school. Those who hold teaching positions concurrently within the school should not receive concurrent salaries.

(3) The school's research institute has only 12 students, but 48 staff members, and spends 3,800 yuan per month. There is no special equipment, and there are no achievements to speak of since its establishment. The research institute should be suspended from the next academic year, and the original funds should be transferred to enrich the equipment of the undergraduate program.

(4) The school's purpose is to cultivate teachers for secondary schools. The cultivation of students' character is especially important compared to other schools. In the future, the school should pay special attention to moral education.

Private Yenching University

Most of the school's teachers are full-time and able to work hard in research. The staff is also conscientious in their work. The allocation of funds is appropriate, and the equipment is adequate. The school provides housing for teachers and staff, giving teachers and students more opportunities to interact. All these achievements are commendable. However, the following points still need attention and improvement:

(1) The school originally had three colleges, eighteen departments, and two specialized courses, as well as a graduate school divided into twelve disciplines, which is too large. The school's current financial resources are difficult, and it should seek to shrink in the following two points to remedy the situation: 1. The colleges and departments should consider merging themselves and submit them to the Ministry for approval. 2. The graduate school should reduce the scope and follow the Ministry's promulgated Provisional Organizational Regulations for University Graduate Schools and submit them for approval.

(2) The school's administration and printed regulations are mostly issued in English, which is inappropriate. In the future, they should be changed to Chinese.

(3) The school's students' lives are mostly extravagant and should be corrected to cultivate a spirit of thrift.

(4) The school's sources of funding have recently been decreasing due to the impact of the world economy, which is a significant shortfall. A determined fund should be raised immediately to consolidate the school's economic foundation.

Private Fu Jen Catholic University in Beiping

Since recent years, the school has been working hard to build new school buildings, add equipment, and determine funding. However, the following points should be followed and improved immediately:

(1) The school originally had three colleges, eleven departments, and preparatory courses, which is too many. They should consider merging themselves and submit them to the Ministry for approval. The pre-medical course was ordered to be canceled by the Ministry of Education a long time ago and should be discontinued immediately, and the students of the course should be merged into the departments of the College of Science.

(2) The school's graduate school should reduce its scope and follow the Provisional Organizational Regulations for University Graduate Schools promulgated by the Ministry of Education three years ago and submit them to the Ministry for approval.

In addition to the organization and description, other departments are all missing. A detailed curriculum outline and content description for each department should be properly formulated and implemented.

(4) The school's teachers mostly hold concurrent positions, and those who are called full-time teachers actually hold part-time teaching positions outside the school, which is inappropriate. Full-time teachers should be hired as much as possible, and part-time teaching outside the school should be restricted.

Private China College

The summarized report states that many aspects of its operation are not in compliance. This college receives a substantial amount of public funding each year, yet there is no demonstrated achievement. This greatly betrays the government's intention in subsidizing private schools. The following is an excerpt of the key points of the report, and it is expected that they will be strictly followed and implemented for improvement:

(1) There are too few science books in the science department, and newly published ones are especially rare. There are only two or three magazines, and they are insignificant. The content of the biology department is somewhat outdated. The equipment is only sufficient for teaching experiments in the lower grades. Advanced physics laboratories are completely lacking. The chemistry instrument and reagent room is very rudimentary. The library and practical equipment of other departments are also makeshift and insufficient for application. The college shall, starting from the next academic year, designate two-thirds of the annual government subsidy, amounting to 80,000 yuan, specifically for the purchase of instruments and books, and report the details of the equipment purchased each semester for review. In addition, the college should raise its own substantial funding to make up for the deficiencies.

(2) Many faculty and staff members hold multiple positions, and even those who are supposed to be full-time often hold other positions elsewhere. The key responsible personnel cannot be on campus daily. Moreover, most of the science faculty members lack the academic qualifications and experience to adequately fulfill their roles. In the future, all staff members, especially key responsible personnel, should be changed to full-time positions. Instructors should be replaced as much as possible with personnel who can reliably and competently fulfill their responsibilities, with full-time employment as the guiding principle.

(3) Students live off-campus, which has a negative impact on moral education and academic atmosphere. It is imperative to add dormitories and require all students to live on campus to improve discipline and promote academic research. In addition, existing students should receive rigorous training, and new students should be rigorously admitted to raise the academic level. (4) This Ministry previously ordered that the physics and chemistry departments of the college be divided into two departments. However, according to the report, the professors and equipment of each department make it difficult to operate as two departments. The scope should be reduced immediately, and the college should consider temporarily establishing one department (either physics or chemistry) and submit a plan to the Ministry for approval. As for the Department of Law, the Economics and Commerce departments should be merged starting from the next academic year.

Private Chaoyang College

The points that the college should improve are presented as follows:

Although the college's buildings are spacious, some classrooms are rectangular in shape, which hinders students' viewing and listening. The location of the library is also unsuitable and needs to be improved urgently. Most of the books in the library are outdated, and Western books are especially rare. An amount should be designated from the college's foundation for the purchase of books.

The college's regular income relies heavily on student fees, which is not a sustainable plan. It is imperative to find other reliable sources of income to ensure stability.

In the past, the college's admissions were not strict, and the number of students was excessive, while the equipment was insufficient. In the future, efforts should be made to reduce enrollment and strictly comply with the Ministry's recent regulations on admissions. The specialized department should be closed in accordance with previous orders.

Many of the college's faculty and staff hold multiple positions, and even those who are supposed to be full-time still hold other positions elsewhere. In the future, instructors should be replaced with personnel who can reliably and competently fulfill their responsibilities, with full-time employment as the guiding principle.

The college lacks statistics on teacher absences, student absences, student withdrawals, and leaves of absence. More than a month after the semester began, students could still register at any time without any restrictions. Entrance examination papers have been completely discarded. Most students live off-campus, and management is lax, which shows a lack of seriousness in both teaching and moral education. All of these issues should be strictly rectified.

In addition, the curriculum of the college's law department relies heavily on lecture notes, which is considered too shallow. In the future, efforts should be made to improve students' ability to read Chinese and Western reference books and cultivate students' spirit of independent research.

Private Peiping Republic College

In the past year, the college has made considerable efforts to improve various aspects. The following key points are presented to order serious improvement:

Most of the college's faculty members are part-time, and their salaries are low. Although the equipment has been slightly increased, it is still insufficient for teaching and reference. All efforts should be made to hire full-time professors, increase their salaries, and enrich various facilities.

The college's fundraising plan is indeed a fundamental solution to improve various undertakings. However, of the 500,000 yuan of funds to be raised, in addition to the 150,000 yuan already stored, the remaining amount should continue to be raised according to the original plan. In addition, raising student levels and enriching the content of academic disciplines are also the college's urgent priorities. Matters such as strict admission of new students, rigorous training of existing students, strict examinations, elimination of unnecessary subjects, and strict scheduling of curriculum should be implemented strenuously.

Private Peiping Union Medical College

The college has excellent facilities and equipment, rich content, and highly qualified faculty and staff members who are all full-time and dedicated to research. The establishment of scholarships, loan programs, and student service departments greatly benefits diligent and excellent students. This is highly commendable. However, the college should improve the following points to maximize its effectiveness:

(1) Given the college's excellent facilities and faculty, the college should consider adding classes as recommended in the report, or making other appropriate arrangements, to enroll more students and broaden the scope of education.

(2) The college's enrollment of new students is limited to students from a small number of public and private universities, which is considered too narrow. Efforts should be made to expand the scope in the future. Furthermore, St. John's University, which is recognized by the college, has not been approved by the Ministry, and students from that school should not be admitted to the college. (3) The college's teaching is excessively focused on English and should be gradually corrected appropriately. In administrative matters, the language used should be primarily Chinese.

(4) The college should strive to cultivate a simple and pragmatic style so that students can better adapt to serving society after graduation.

Private Railway College

Since the college was approved by the Ministry, it has paid attention to implementing the improvement guidelines. However, the college's curriculum lacks standards and should be detailed and strictly implemented. New and important books and magazines should also be purchased as appropriate. The number of part-time faculty members should be reduced and more full-time faculty members should be hired, and their salaries should be increased. Key staff members should be prohibited from holding positions outside the college. Furthermore, the academic level of the college's students is low. In the future, the admission of new students should be strict, and current students should receive diligent training. (End)

Graduation Qualifications for Students Taking the Joint Examination in This City

Verified and approved after checking academic records.

Those whose academic records do not match shall be dealt with according to law.

The joint graduation examination for middle schools in this city was held for three days starting on June 25th. The examination papers for each subject have been graded separately. All joint examination results will be announced today. However, the graduation qualifications of students participating in this year's joint examination whose academic records have not been verified will be determined after the transfer documents have been verified. The Municipal Bureau of Education issued a special announcement yesterday stating that since the Bureau changed the method of verifying academic records, the academic records of all students from other schools who transfer to schools in this city are verified by the school in this city sending the documents directly to the competent educational administrative organ in the location of the student's original school, and then the verifying organ directly replies to this Bureau to verify whether their academic qualifications match in order to determine whether to approve or reject. Many of the students from middle schools in this city who participated in this year's joint graduation examination have not yet had their responses from the competent educational administrative organs in the location of the original school sent to the Bureau. In addition to allowing them to participate in the joint examination first, the graduation qualifications of these students will still be determined after the academic records have been verified and sent to the Bureau. Those whose academic records are found to be inconsistent or who have forged documents shall be dealt with according to law. This is hereby announced for public knowledge.

In addition, in this year's graduation examination, 951 students from 50 schools who passed all subjects are approved for graduation, and 1,612 students from 72 junior high schools who passed all subjects are approved for graduation.

Results of the Joint Examination for Middle Schools in Beijing Announced

Nanjing, 14th telegram) The results of the joint graduation examination for middle schools in Beijing were announced on the 14th. A total of 1,449 senior and junior high school students participated. 612 junior high school students passed, 301 students who failed one or two subjects were allowed to advance, and 73 students failed. 220 senior high school students passed, 121 students who failed one or two subjects were allowed to advance, and 149 students failed. In addition, the elementary school section has also been graded. Of the 1,405 students, 1,321 passed and 84 failed. Graduation certificates have been issued by the Bureau of Social Affairs for college and university entrance examination.

Shandong Province Middle School Joint Examination Results Announced

Pass rate accounts for 77%

Retention rate accounts for 7.3%

Science has improved, Chinese and Party Principles are relatively poor

(Jinan, 14th telegram) The results of the provincial middle school joint examination were announced today. 1,575 students passed, accounting for 77% of the total number of examinees. Retention rate accounts for only 7.3%. 16% of students who failed two subjects will have a make-up exam, which is an improvement over the previous two sessions. 7 students who scored above 90 points will be awarded book coupons of less than 100 yuan separately. Science has improved, while Chinese and Party Principles are relatively poor.

The Annual Meeting of the China Vocational Education Society Opens in Gan

357 representatives from 25 provinces and cities attended. The proposals are divided into improving rural and remedial education curricula, etc. The opening ceremony was grand. Chairman Chiang Kai-shek personally wrote a training speech. (Nanchang correspondent) The 4th Annual Meeting of the China Vocational Education Society and the 12th National Vocational Education Discussion Conference were held at 9:00 a.m. on the 13th in the Siqi Hall of the Jiangxi Provincial Department of Education. Attendees included 357 representatives from 25 provinces and cities, including Jilin and Qingdao, and more than 200 guests, including Central Committee member Ding Chaowu, Executive Headquarters representative Wen Qun, the Provincial Government Secretary-General, Director Cheng of the Education Department, and Ministry of Education representative Zhong Zhixiu. After the meeting, Chairman Jiang Wenyu led the attendees in paying their respects before delivering a training speech. Then, Huang Yanpei delivered a speech. Wen Qun read Chairman Chiang Kai-shek's handwritten training speech sent from Lushan. Then, Central Committee member Ding Chaowu, Ministry of Education representative Zhong, and other guests delivered speeches one after another. The ceremony ended at 12:00. The General Assembly discussed proposals in the afternoon. The details are as follows.

25 Provinces and Cities

Guangdong, Guangxi, Jiangsu, Zhejiang, Shaanxi, Gansu, Hunan, Hubei, Henan, Anhui, Fujian, Shandong, Jilin, Sichuan, Yunnan, Guizhou, Hebei, Suiyuan, Jiangxi, and other 20 provinces, Guangzhou, Hangzhou, Shanghai, Qingdao, Peiping and other 5 cities, members and representatives Jiang Wenyu, Huang Yanpei, and others, 357 people.

Chiang's Written Training Speech

It is common knowledge that education is the fundamental undertaking for national salvation. Among various types of education, vocational education is most in line with today's needs and is especially recognized by the gentlemen of your society. Your society has been promoting vocational education for many years with the power of the masses, and the achievements are indeed considerable, which is worthy of our admiration. However, there is one thing that the gentlemen must pay attention to, that is, from a superficial observation, most people in our country are suffering from unemployment, while a small number of employed people lack the skills to meet the requirements of their jobs. Therefore, only by developing vocational education can we reduce the past education system's drawback of producing high-level idlers, and enable those who have jobs to be competent and those who have careers to enjoy their work. However, if we make a more in-depth observation, we will know that the people of the country do not suffer from lack of jobs, but from lack of responsibility to be loyal to their jobs, and do not suffer from lack of skills to meet the requirements of their jobs, but from lack of ambition to seek progress. To remedy this shortcoming, it seems that the promotion of vocational education alone cannot be successful. In recent months, Zhongzheng launched the New Life Movement, and its purpose is also to be here. I deeply hope that the gentlemen understand this point, and must infuse the spirit of the New Life Movement into vocational education. In other words, the people must understand etiquette, righteousness, integrity, and shame, and then vocational education can be fully effective. Now that your society is gathering in Nanchang, I will specially offer a few words as a contribution. Chiang Kai-shek, July 13th

The 4th Annual Meeting of the Chinese Statistical Society Opens Today

Liu Dajun, Wang Zhongwu, and others were elected as directors

Banquet invited Cai Yuanpei and others to attend this afternoon

The Chinese Statistical Society held a social affairs meeting yesterday morning, and a joint banquet was held by five groups at noon. In the afternoon, papers were read at the New Asia Auditorium, and the Economic Research Office of the Bank of China held a public banquet at 7:00 p.m. The social affairs meeting will continue this morning, and papers will be read. A banquet will be held for various groups at noon, and the meeting will be closed at 2:00 p.m. The details are recorded as follows.

Social Affairs Meeting

The social affairs meeting was held on the ninth floor of the Youth Association at 9:00 a.m. Dozens of people attended, including Wang Zhongwu, Wu Dajun, Sheng Zhuosan, Cai Zhengya, and Zhu Junyi. President Wang Zhongwu chaired the meeting. The Chinese Shorthand Research Society sent a member to record. After the rituals, the president reported on the general situation of social affairs. (1) Members: The society has 188 members, an increase of 29 over the previous session. Among these 29 people, 16 are university professors, and the rest are engaged in statistical work in the central and local governments. (1) Work achievements: (A) Research on the naming and segmentation standards of arithmetic consulted by the National Compilation and Translation Museum. (B) Organize the Population Survey Research Committee and investigate the population survey methods in various important provinces and cities. (C) Publish the Statistical Review. (D) Solicit books for members to read. (E) Investigate the recent situation of members and publish a list of the society. (F) Review statistical terms. Chen Changheng then reported on the work of the Population Survey Research Committee, and Zhu Junyi reported on the work of the Terminology Review Committee.

Discussion Proposals

After the report, the proposals were discussed. (A) Proposals from members of the social affairs committee. (1) The social affairs committee system of the society is proposed to be changed to a director system to conform to the legal system of mass groups. The resolution was passed. (2) Revise "Ordinary members who pay ten years of social fees are permanently exempt from fees" to "Permanent members of this society to show excellence." The resolution was passed. (3) Create a Statistical Journal. The resolution was passed. (4) Raise the society's foundation and build houses in the capital to seek the development of social affairs. The resolution was handed over to the next session of the social affairs meeting for handling. (5) Member proposals. (1) Yang Shouliang proposed to organize a statistical talent introduction committee to introduce relevant statistical talents to various domestic institutions and seek appropriate jobs for members of the society. (Liu Shaoqian proposed to correct the pronunciation of "shi" to distinguish it from "dan" to facilitate statistics. The resolution was passed in principle and handed over to the next session of staff for consideration. (C) Revise the society's constitution.

Election of Directors

The meeting used the postal election method. The votes were counted yesterday, and as a result, Liu Dajun, Zhongwu, Zhu Junyi, Wu Dajun, Cai Zhengya, Zhang Xinyi, Jin Guobao and other seven people were elected as directors, and Chen Changheng, He Lian, and Chu Yifei and other three people were elected as alternate directors. After the election, a photo was taken and the meeting was adjourned.

Public Banquet Situation

After the social affairs meeting, the Pacific International Society, Jiaotong University Research Institute, China Economic Statistics Research Institute, Banking Society Social and Economic Survey Institute and other five groups held a banquet for the society's members at the New Asia Hotel. A total of more than 60 people attended, including He Dekui of the China Economic Statistics Research Institute, Ke Chengmao of the Jiaotong University Research Institute, Liu Yuwan of the Pacific International Society, the Social and Economic Survey Institute, and the society's members. During the banquet, He Dekui and others gave welcome speeches on behalf of the group, and Wu Dajun of the Chinese Statistical Society gave a reply speech on behalf of the society.

Reading Papers

In the afternoon, papers were read at the New Asia Auditorium. The reader was Liu Dajun, chairman of the Paper Committee. More than ten papers from members were received this time. Wang Zhongwu's "Discussion on the Specific Plan for the Chinese Population Survey" is detailed and will make a great contribution to the government's general survey of the Chinese population in the future. The outline is recorded as follows. (1) The meaning of the population census. (2) The scope of the object of the population census. (3) The date and time of the survey. (4) Survey methods. (5) Survey matters. (6) Survey forms. (7) Division of survey area. (8) Organization of survey agency. (9) Personnel and training. (10) Survey expenses. (11) Data collation. (12) Conclusion.

Today's Closing Ceremony

Today, from 9:00 to 10:00 AM, papers will be read and a social affairs meeting will be held. At 12:30 PM, the society will host a banquet at the New Asia Hotel, to which Central Committee member Cai Yuanpei, Mayor Wu, and bureau chiefs from various municipal departments have been invited to attend. The closing ceremony will take place at 2:00 PM this afternoon.

Zhang Shouyong and Qiu Hanping Establish China Maritime Vocational School

Yesterday's Press Conference on School's Mission and Policies

The private China Maritime Vocational School, located at 233 Metcalfe Road in this city, was founded by Zhang Shouyong, Qiu Hanping, and others, as previously reported in this newspaper. Yesterday, at Zhang's residence in the India Curry Restaurant on Sima Road, a reception was held for reporters from various newspapers to report on the school's mission and their own policies for running the school. Zhang began by stating that in recent years, economic panic has caused a slump in all industries, and that internal and external troubles are pressing in on all sides. The people's livelihoods are becoming increasingly difficult. After graduation, young students find it difficult to find employment, which may lead to shortsightedness or dangerous paths. Farmers and workers are abandoning their villages and entering the cities. If this continues, it will not be a long-term solution. To save the current crisis, the whole country is urgently focused on rural revitalization. However, rural revitalization cannot be achieved by empty talk. It must be deeply rooted in the countryside. Therefore, training talent is the most urgent task. When engaging in rural construction, we should first pay attention to the relationship between cities and rural areas. Today, China's finances are concentrated in the cities, while the countryside is extremely poor. The best way to channel funds from cities into rural areas is to promote credit cooperatives. Credit cooperatives in cities can meet the urgent needs of wage earners and channel surplus funds from cities into rural areas. England, France, Germany, Denmark, and other countries have been doing this for years with remarkable results, which we can learn from. This is the first goal of establishing this school. Young students are often at a loss after graduation, and school authorities only consider their responsibility fulfilled by issuing graduation certificates. The graduates' future paths and social guidance are completely ignored. Such education can only be called the responsibility of "teaching," and the word "education" is not fully realized. This is acceptable in ordinary schools, but not in vocational education. Not only are parents greatly disappointed, but young students will also have short-sighted ideas. Therefore, vocational education must fully realize the two characters of education, especially since teaching must include nurturing. With this in mind, the school strives to enrich students' knowledge during their studies so that they can take on work in the future. After graduation, it helps them find employment. If they cannot find employment, the school will be responsible for their living expenses. This graduation employment plan has been thoroughly researched by Mr. Qiu Hanping, who has concrete plans, and the school is confident that it can be achieved. In this way, vocational school graduates will not become an unemployed mass, which aligns with the true meaning of vocational education. This is the second goal of establishing this school. What is learned is not what is used, and what is used is not what is learned. This is a common problem in China today. The courses offered by schools are often ambitious and impractical. Young students spend a long time idling and developing bad habits at school. Therefore, even if they have a job after graduation, it is difficult for them to be competent. I firmly believe that young people with both good character and academic performance who are hardworking and able to endure hardship will not have to worry about unemployment. We should also pay attention to students' character and practical knowledge when providing education. The establishment of this school is intended to enable young people to seek practical knowledge and skills, as well as physical and mental training, for the benefit of themselves and others in the future. This is the third goal of establishing this school. However, the school is still in its initial stage, with a small scale, and needs the support and guidance of everyone, and so on. Finally, Principal Qiu Hanping described the process of establishing the school and the future direction. It is reported that dozens of applications are received daily from outside the city, and the school will hold its first entrance examination on the 23rd of this month.

Chinese Culture Society Shanghai Branch Holds Public Education

Implementation Begins in Caojiadu

Since its establishment, the Shanghai Branch of the Chinese Culture Society has been working with extraordinary intensity. In addition to publishing various magazines and series to engage in academic movements, it has also begun to promote public education. Through the efforts of committee members Liu Bingli, Xiao Zuolin, Ni Wenya, Chen Gaimin, and Xu Jin, and with the support of Mayor Wu Tiecheng, a public school has been officially established in Caojiadu. The school focuses on three goals: teaching illiterate people the basic characters used in daily life, teaching illiterate people simple living knowledge and skills, and enabling illiterate people to recognize the importance of national, state, and group life. A thousand-character textbook has been compiled for students to study. To meet the needs of workers, classes are divided into day and night shifts. Students who study at the school for two hours can also receive rice coupons worth five cents. Therefore, the number of students enrolled has reached over a thousand, and latecomers have a sense of regret. It is learned that the school held its opening ceremony at the Caojiadu Zhongyi Association on the evening of the 11th. Over a thousand guests attended, including Xu Jin, Chairman, Liu Bingli, Xiao Zuolin, Ni Wenya, Directors of the Cultural Society, Ruan Jue, Director of the China Industrial and Commercial Rubber Factory, Zhang Zhedian, and other guests who delivered speeches in succession, followed by the screening of movies produced by the Star and Tianyi Film Companies.

Baihong Track and Field Team Holds Memorial Service for Sun Duoqi

9:00 AM This Morning at the Jingwu Athletic Association

The Baihong Track and Field Team will hold a memorial service for the team's late Secretary-General, Mr. Sun Duoqi, at the auditorium of the Jingwu Athletic Association on North Sichuan Road, Hengbang Bridge, this morning at 9:00 AM. The various details are recorded below.

A Brief Biography of Sun Duoqi Mr. Sun Duoqi was a native of Shouchun, Anhui. He worked at the Shanghai Postal Administration. In 1920, indignant about China's disastrous defeat at the Far Eastern Games, he organized the Baihong Track and Field Team with Chen Xuzhou, Chen Baoqiu, Wang Jianwu, and others. Mr. Sun was elected as the Secretary-General and worked diligently, sparing no effort for five years. Baihong was able to develop thanks to him. Recently, he planned for Baihong to go north to participate in the Suzhou Triangle Competition. Unfortunately, he fell ill and passed away suddenly. When Baihong went to Suzhou to participate in the Triangle Competition, they were shocked to hear the sad news. The entire army wept and wore black gauze on their arms to express their condolences. The depth of their feelings was such.

The Memorial Service Ceremony The memorial service will follow the following ceremony: (1) Opening Ceremony (2) Playing of Mournful Music (Postal Military Band) (3) All Stand in Silence and Bow Three Times to Mr. Sun Duoqi's Portrait (4) Three Minutes of Silence (5) Presentation of Flowers (6) Reading of the Eulogy (7) Report (8) Speech (9) Thank You Speech (10) Playing of Music and Closing Ceremony The Staff of the Memorial Service The staff have been appointed as follows: (Presiding Officiant) Chen Xuzhou (Assistant Officiant) Li Minxun, (Master of Ceremonies) Lao Boshi, Kang Kongzhao, (Reception) Xu Duo, Gu Huiyuan, Sun Huipei, Mao Honggui, Gu Yingfu, Huang Shengbai (Staff) Zhu Jianggu, Chen Ninglin, Xu Yanbo, Yu Cunyao

Tennis New Techniques (5)

J. PARMLY PARET Original Work, Joint Translation by Qian Yiqin and Hong Jun, All Rights Reserved, Reproduction Prohibited

Not only must the heels not touch the ground, but the knees must also be slightly bent, so that the movements can be flexible and free. A player who can quickly respond to the overall situation on the court has already achieved half of their success. Because in order to meet balls coming from any direction and be prepared to reach them in time, the entire body weight must always be kept in a downward-sitting posture.

Regarding the above three basic rules—that is, both feet are parallel to the flight path of the ball, the heels do not touch the ground, and the knees are slightly bent—after understanding them, now let's go back to study the relationship between the position of the feet and the net, the position the body should take for the flight path of the ball and good shots. To move quickly, you must use the foot farthest in the direction you want to move to push off. Therefore, when both feet are parallel to the net, moving left and right becomes very fast, because one foot or the other is always in a relative position, and when quick action is needed, one of the feet can naturally serve as a support. However, in reality, there are many times when the feet need to move forward, backward, or diagonally. At this time, if both feet are standing flat, you lose support and cannot move quickly. To move forward or backward, one foot must be quickly moved in front of or behind the other foot, and then the body can actually move forward or backward. From this, it can be seen that before hitting the ball, the most appropriate position is for both feet to be at an angle to the net. For forehand or backhand shots, the feet must move very quickly, so standing with both feet flat is impossible. Experienced players do not need to run to meet balls that can be reached; they always wait for the ball to fly close to their body and simply step their feet quickly into the appropriate position to respond freely. Because both feet are standing diagonally, there is absolutely no restriction on moving forward, backward, left, or right, and no time is wasted, and the movement of the feet is very fast, which is a very important point.

If the ball comes to the right side, then of course a forehand shot should be used. If the ball's bounce is strong at this time, move the right foot behind the left foot; if the ball's bounce is weak, move the left foot forward. Conversely, if the ball comes to the left side, then of course a backhand shot should be used. If the right foot is moved forward to meet a short bounce, then the left foot is moved backward to meet a long bounce. When shooting forward, the body should rotate from the hips, and the head of the racket should meet the incoming ball to increase the force of the impact. When the racket swings backward, the entire body weight is concentrated on the right foot and leg, and then the leg moves forward to shoot, shifting the weight to the left foot (this is in regards to a forehand shot; for a backhand shot, the two feet are reversed). The racket should still reach the end point, but the player's body must still maintain balance.

The player's eyes, of course, absolutely must be focused on the ball. "Keep your eyes on the ball" is the slogan for success in tennis. From the beginning of the game until the end, the eyes must not leave the ball. The slightest inattention will inevitably lead to mistakes. Therefore, when hitting the ball, to ensure both the speed and direction are effective, the eyes must be focused on the ball. This is a basic rule that beginners must not neglect.

This foot movement to respond to incoming balls must be extremely fast and convenient. Therefore, when waiting for an incoming ball, having both feet angled towards the net is much more convenient and flexible for foot movement than having both feet standing flat towards the net. When hitting the ball, slightly squatting the body forward has significant benefits. Body weight must follow the racket forward to increase the power of the shot. When the racket swings forward, straightening the body from the slightly squatting position can strengthen the power of the shot. With the body slightly squatting forward, the knees are naturally slightly bent, so when the racket hits, the body straightens up, and the force of the body weight, in this situation, must follow the racket out, thus increasing the racket's momentum and the power of the shot.

When both feet are standing in the appropriate position, the hips should be slightly turned to the side, like playing golf. During the shot, the hips naturally follow the racket and turn to the front. Thus, the combined power of the bent legs, the shifting hips, and the body weight leaning, plus the power of the arm from the shoulder to the wrist on the racket, becomes a huge concentrated force. All experienced players are good at using this concentrated force to direct the ball to the opponent's area.

The "follow-through" used in playing golf is also an important element of tennis technique. Because after the ball is hit away from the racket, the power of the whole body must still follow the momentum forward and not stop immediately. Beginners often think that as long as the ball leaves the racket, it's over and they can stop exerting force, which is very dangerous. You need to know that although the propulsive force cannot affect the ball's flight after it leaves the racket, if there is a tendency to stop pushing forward as soon as the racket is swung out before or during the shot, it will affect the power of the shot itself and cause changes, and will also indirectly affect the ball's flight.

Women's World, Issue 22

In Memory of Martyr Qiu Jin

— Editor

Reading the report from Anqing City in this newspaper on the 6th of this month, I learned that Anhui Province held the 27th anniversary commemoration of Xu Xilin's martyrdom at the Provincial Party Headquarters on that day, and the provincial government stipulated that July 6th every year would be Anqing Memorial Day. This news of honoring the martyrs couldn't help but comfort Martyr Xu in the afterlife, but at the same time, it grieved me for another martyr.

Who is the other martyr? Needless to say, it is Qiu Jin.

Ms. Qiu and Martyr Xu had the same ideals, the same plans, the same actions, and the same relationship in their martyrdom. However, one is mourned by ten thousand people, while the other only has tangled weeds scattered around the door. How can this contrast not make people regretful?

Ms. Qiu's life deeds are clearly visible to everyone. Her lonely tomb can make the mountains and lakes magnificent, but now the wind and rain pavilion next to the tomb has been destroyed by wind and rain, only making passersby feel a sense of desolation. I remember the statue of Mr. Chen Qimei, a martyr of Zhejiang Province, standing majestically in Hangzhou's Hubin Park, and the memorial day of Mr. Zhu Zhixin, with memorial ceremonies held by all agencies in the province. The martyrs sacrificed themselves for the country and did not count the posthumous honors. However, from the perspective of respecting the spirit of the martyrs, I really feel that people like Ms. Qiu

deserve to be given a memorial day like other martyrs, to receive people's admiration and love.

The day this issue of our publication is published is exactly the anniversary of Ms. Qiu's martyrdom (two days before June 6th of the lunar calendar). We have specially prepared a few short articles to express a small token of remembrance and to encourage our female compatriots to know the way to aspire.

Thoughts on Commemorating the Female Knight Qiu Jin

— Ji Qun

Today, twenty-seven years ago, was the day the Female Knight Qiu Jin of Jianhu was arrested. The country in which Ms. Qiu lived was the Qing Empire, which was being bullied by powerful neighbors and had a corrupt internal administration. The society in which Ms. Qiu lived was a feudal society. The family in which Ms. Qiu lived was an old-fashioned patriarchal family. However, Ms. Qiu was able to transcend everything and die for family revolution, racial revolution, and even social revolution. Not only is her spirit of sacrifice enough to encourage the weak and establish the timid, but judging from her talent and ideas, she is also a rare talent in history. Today, as we commemorate her, we should recognize the following aspects of her:

First, when women's education had not yet flourished, Ms. Qiu was in an old-fashioned family. She was able to avoid being swallowed by patriarchal ideology. In addition to studying old books, she read extensively in Chinese and foreign newspapers and absorbed ideas from all aspects to complete her own revolutionary propositions. This spirit of studiousness and deep thinking is truly commendable.

Second, Ms. Qiu was married to a man surnamed Wang and had children. Because she felt the pain of inequality between men and women, she was able to avoid being bound by feudal ideology, disregarded everything to leave her family, and went abroad to study alone. She resolutely joined the Tongmenghui (Revolutionary Alliance) founded by Mr. Sun Yat-sen and engaged in revolutionary activities with her comrades. This brave revolutionary spirit is not only rare for ordinary women, but also not easy for those who call themselves revolutionaries.

Third, after Ms. Qiu returned to China from Japan, she founded the China Women's News and ran the Mingdao Women's School in order to save the two hundred million women from male oppression, seeking the true liberation of women. At the same time, she presided over the Datong Sports Association founded by Xu Xilin. She compiled the Restoration Army and the Dare-to-Die Corps to lead the revolution with action. This practical and striving spirit is by no means comparable to those who merely talk about liberation and revolution.

From the above facts, we know that Ms. Qiu's personality is great, her insights are outstanding, her thoughts are advanced, and her actions are brave. Ms. Qiu's implementation of the revolution was in the hope of overthrowing the corrupt Qing government and achieving enlightened governance and a reasonable society. Ms. Qiu's advocacy of women's education and equal rights between men and women was to give women the opportunity to study and be independent, and to achieve equal status with men. She said that the cause was difficult and would take decades to achieve its goals. Indeed, more than twenty years later, women's education is prevalent and men and women are equal. However, what is the personality, status, and ability of women? All we see are six batches of "[square hat]" ornaments that can only consume and cannot produce being manufactured in various schools every year; all we see are disturbing news about rape, abandonment, suicide, and demands for alimony being revealed in various newspapers! To seek talents like Ms. Qiu who strive to transform the personal environment, the social environment, and the national environment, it seems that I have not yet discovered any, with my narrow knowledge. This is worthy of deep reflection by women's circles—especially on this day of commemorating Ms. Qiu!

About Qiu Jin the Poet

— Chong Hen

Qiu Jin was originally a poet, but her status as a poet was overshadowed by her career. As long as we dissect Qiu Jin's life trajectory, we can see that she exudes the temperament of a poet everywhere. Her chivalry, her generous and tragic songs, and her dissatisfaction with her original background all prove that she possesses the romantic essence of a poet. Needless to say, her last words at the time of her sacrifice, the words that used the line of poetry "[Autumn rain and autumn wind sadden people to death]" to replace her confession, fully displayed her life as a poet.

Qiu Jin was born in the late Qing Dynasty, her era was when imperialism began to reach out to China, and it was also when Chinese national thought began to open its eyes. A series of events in her era were: the Sino-Japanese War, the Hundred Days' Reform, and the Boxer Rebellion. This inevitably made her keenly aware that the ruling class had to be overthrown. Being on the eve of the Xinhai Revolution, she was even more pushed by the actual movements of the time and increasingly wanted to rise up and do the work of: national salvation. In this way, her revolutionary life was formed, and at the same time, her swan song of poetry was produced.

Her poetry can be said to be especially outstanding among the always small number of female poets in China. As long as we flip through her posthumous collection, we can find that in her poems and lyrics

A Brief Account of Qiu Jin's Life

— Bi Yao

It has been a full twenty-seven years since Ms. Qiu Jin's martyrdom. Her life deeds have all become obvious historical traces. However, the editors of this publication believe that Ms. Qiu's spirit—the revolutionary spirit—should be re-emphasized, so before the anniversary of her martyrdom is near, they asked me to write this manuscript. Unfortunately, on the day of Ms. Qiu's martyrdom, I was far away in the remote mountains playing with a group of children, and I did not know her appearance or actions at all. Years ago, when I traveled to Hangzhou, I often interacted with Ms. Xu Xiaoshu, Ms. Qiu's highly talented student, and only then did I get some general ideas.

Ms. Qiu's name is Jin. An Xuanqing, styled herself as the Female Knight of Jianhu, a native of Shanyin County, Zhejiang. Her father was an official who gave birth to her in Fujian; later he was transferred to Hunan, and he betrothed her to a wealthy gentleman surnamed Wang in Xiangtan as his daughter-in-law, and she bore one son and one daughter. She lived with the Wang family in Beijing for many years. The Hundred Days' Reform and the Boxer Rebellion gave her unlimited stimulation. She wanted to break out of the boudoir and the family, and take on the heavy responsibility of saving the country. At this time, she wrote in a [Man Jiang Hong] ci poem:

Staying briefly in Jinghua, it is already the Mid-Autumn Festival. For the chrysanthemums blooming all over the fence, the autumn scenery is like wiping. The four sides are broken by the remnants of Chu, and the eight years of flavor are missed from Zhejiang. I am forced to be made an eyebrow, but I am not willing. I cannot be listed as a man, but my heart is fiercer than a man's. My life's loyalty is always heated because of people. Who recognizes my vulgar breast? The hero's last road should be tempered. Where can I find a confidant in the red dust? My green shirt is wet.

Within her social circle of official families, there were, of course, some vulgar people who tasted their conscience and enjoyed wealth and honor. Where else could there be figures who cared about the rise and fall of the country? Therefore, she had to sigh deeply that [where can I find a confidant in the red dust], and even cried and wept, her green shirt completely soaked.

But when the time came, she finally decided to break through this mediocre and dim environment, break through the shackles of women crouching under the old ethics; she flew far away and went to Japan to study.

The matter happened like this; in a certain month of the 30th year of Guangxu, a revolutionary newcomer was arrested and imprisoned in Beijing. Everyone knows that the official prisons of the Qing Dynasty had many places where money could be used to get things done. Our enthusiastic Ms. Qiu, who loved the country and admired the revolution, had her loyalty that was always heated for people greatly boiling. She took off her own hairpins and ornaments and secretly sent six hundred yuan for the release movement fee for that unknown prisoner. This incident ignited the anger of the man surnamed Wang, and the two made a big commotion. She abandoned her family and boarded a ship to Japan. The man surnamed Wang was so anxious that he chased her to the shipyard and demanded the Wang family's belongings from her. She threw the only luggage, the brocade quilt, from the bow of the ship. In this way, she breathed the fresh air of the Pacific Ocean. At this time, Mr. Sun Yat-sen was organizing the Tongmenghui (Revolutionary Alliance) in Tokyo, Japan, and Ms. Qiu was the first to join. She also introduced many comrades from Jiangsu and Zhejiang to join the party. Whenever there was a gathering, she would definitely take the stage and give a passionate speech, advocating revolution, which made the Qing government uneasy and secretly told the Japanese to find ways to ban it. The Japanese revised a regulation to crack down on studying abroad, and most of the students returned home in anger. Ms. Qiu was one of them. The Wang family had a father who heard that she had returned to the country and insisted that she return to Hunan. Because the party army was in economic difficulties, she also took the plan to count. When she got there, she pretended to owe a lot of debts outside, and the old man gave them all to her, but he was very strict in guarding against her actions.

One day, she said she was going to the temple to watch a play, and the family saw that she had dressed the children neatly and brought them along, so they didn't suspect anything. Unexpectedly, she sat in a sedan chair to the theater, settled the children on the stage, and flew away.

Returning to Jiangsu and Zhejiang, she taught at Xunxi Women's School in Nanxun. Soon she went to Shanghai to preside over the Tongmenghui's communication agency, and often made explosives. Once, the medicine exploded and she almost faced danger. At the same time, she published the China Women's News, inside which was a publication speech that was truly clangorous and moving. In the 33rd year of Guangxu, she returned to Shaoxing to preside over the Mingdao Women's School. Because Xu Xilin had already aspired to enter Anhui, he entrusted the Datong Sports Association that he had run in Shaoxing entirely to Ms. Qiu. This association had content and was purely preparing for revolutionary military affairs, compiling the eight armies of [Restoring the Han Nationality and Greatly Revitalizing National Power], called the Restoration Army. In May of this year, it had been roughly formed, waiting for Xu Xilin to start an uprising in Anhui, and she would respond in Zhejiang.

On May 25th, Xu Xilin assassinated Governor Enming in Anhui, and was killed after the event failed. At this time, the city was full of wind and rain. Ms. Qiu told her comrades to temporarily avoid it, and she remained in the Datong school. On the night of June 5th, she was finally arrested after being betrayed by a traitor. At first, she was imprisoned in the Shanyin County Office. Because there was no confession, Magistrate Li Zhongyu did not execute her. Shaoxing Prefect Gui Fu was furious, so Magistrate Li sent the entire case to the Prefectural Governor and hanged himself.

Ms. Qiu was usually good at covering up, so she had close relations with Gui Fu. That night, Gui Fu personally interrogated her, asking her if she had any accomplices. She said [Yes]. Gui Fu asked who it was, and she said [It's you]. Gui Fu was so frightened that he dared not ask any further, so he gave her paper and pen and told her to write a confession. She picked up the pen and only wrote the famous poem [Autumn rain and autumn wind sadden people to death]. At 3 a.m. on June 6th, she was killed at Xuanting in Shaoxing Prefecture. Her boiling hot blood, along with the long night, was sprinkled under the cold, autumn-like green blade. She was only thirty-three years old.

She did not see the fall of the Qing Dynasty, nor did she participate in the merits of the Xinhai Revolution. However, was her blood shed in vain? Mr. Tan Sitong did not learn from the escape of Kang Liang and others after the Wuxu coup. At that time, he had a famous saying that [When have you ever seen a successful major reform without bloodshed?] Indeed, the bloodshed of their martyrs was the prelude to the success of the Xinhai Revolution.

Some people believe that Ms. Qiu was only limited to racial revolution, which is a regrettable thing. In fact, this does not harm Ms. Qiu. For a figure of an era, one only needs to be able to be a pioneer of that era, and one cannot demand that he be a pioneer of generations later. If Ms. Qiu was born today, she would have another kind of thought. Looking at her song [Compatriots' Suffering], even when concentrating on the idea of racial revolution, she was already able to pay attention to all aspects of politics and society. The original song has four verses, and two verses are now recorded as follows:

Compatriots' suffering, compatriots' suffering is as bitter as coptis chinensis. The pressure is a thousand pounds and it is difficult to make yourself comfortable. Ghosts and gods wail and are truly pitiful. Alas! The world says tyranny is as fierce as a tiger. When will we see a year of injustice? The sound card is all over the land like a forest. There are hundreds of millions of patrols and officials. Fierce as jackals and poisonous as snakes, they drool at the sight of property. I must, must, must raise troops to sweep away the poisonous fog and see the blue sky. Hand-held white blades search for traitors, and sacrificing lives to save the people is a sage.

Compatriots' suffering, compatriots' suffering is as bitter as coptis chinensis. Whipping compatriots like dogs and horses, the traitors treat themselves like gods. There are smoke paste donations and wine donations, and all kinds of house donations and shop donations. Even the slightest socks and shoes are taken as donations, and not even a single grass or tree is spared. I must, must, must raise troops to sweep away the poisonous fog and see the blue sky. Hand-held white blades search for traitors, and sacrificing lives to save the people is a sage.

In terms of action, her life was to break through the old family, break through the old ethics, and then seek to overthrow the dark alien rule, so that the motherland would gradually prosper. In terms of literature, she also made great achievements. She broke the common practice of ordinary people since the Ming and Qing dynasties of only finding some stale words and rotten characters and desperately putting them together to become poems and lyrics. Her posthumous works are all creative and full of life. Looking at her short life, she did her best in all aspects and showed the spirit of revolution in all aspects.

Today is again the fourth day of the lunar June, standing on the eve of Ms. Qiu's martyrdom anniversary, imagining her singing [Autumn rain and autumn wind sadden people to death] and going to the execution ground with passion and excitement, how can people not wave their fists and dance, and raise their hair and stare, only wanting to rush towards the evil forces and dark circles she encountered?

Apart from a few poems in the early period that were purely chanting personal sadness, most of the other poems and lyrics are overflowing with revolutionary enthusiasm. The beauty of her poems is generally woven from two kinds of thoughts: the first is national thought, and the second is women's rights thought. And these two thoughts are precisely the greatest products of her era.

I believe that when talking about Qiu Jin's poems, one must understand the two kinds of thoughts contained in her poems. Because this is the true value of Qiu Jin, and this is why Qiu Jin is Qiu Jin.

Unfortunately, I don't have [A Collection of the Works of the Female Knight Qiu Jin] at hand, so I can only recall some of her famous lines from memory as follows:

(1) Regarding national thought: There is no way to refine stones to ask Nüwa, and the white horse passes the gap to feel the passing of time. The tragedy of partitioning is close at hand, and shouting is useless. The motherland has a responsibility to sink, and I have no home to wander in the end of the world. A heart full of enthusiasm is sad to look back, and the intestines are broken and it is difficult to be a May flower.

Hearing that the ancient battleground still bears the bloodstains today. The dream of riding horses in the Central Plains, the broken rivers and mountains, shame the old country. There is no right to the territorial waters, so it is sad and lonely. There is a day to sharpen the knife and quickly avenge the hatred. The wind blows coldly, and ten thousand clouds and smoke are collected in the eyes.

I sigh that Shenzhou is sinking, and I am ashamed to steal my life without any plan to save the time. There is a wish to fight for the revival of Chu, and there is no cone to strike against the tyranny of Qin. Only when the country is broken do we know that the human species is cheap, and righteousness is high and does not hinder the poverty of guests. I hate that I have not rewarded my comrades for my business, so I hold my sword and sing sadly with tears in my eyes.

Say return, where to return? Looking back, the motherland is still snoring. Foreign insults are invading, the content is corrupt, and there is no hero to be the master. Alas, God is blind: to see such a country, how can I bear to return to the barbarians? Pea-split melon sharing, all for my homeland.

(2) Regarding women's rights thought

Who is generous and speaks the same hatred? Who recognizes Guo Jie's flow in those days? The current situation is so dangerous, I am willing to exchange Min clothing for Wu hooks. Dirty world, how many men are British and wise? It is only in the ranks of beautiful eyebrows that we occasionally hear of outstanding people: Liangyu's merits and tears on her chest, and Yunying's career and blood in her heart. I drunkenly caress my long sword and make a dragon's chant, the sound is sad and choked. The incense of freedom, I always think of burning it: the hatred of family and country. When will it be vented? Seeing us today, each should work hard. Zhenba must think about settling the species, and prosperity must not only boast of clothing and jue, but the three inches of arched shoes are too useless, and should be reformed!

I hope you will reverse the declining trend and promote solid learning. Lotus tongue with latent splendor, deafening voice. Wake up the sisters of the world, listen to the five watch bells!

On Women (Continued)

— Written by Maxim Gorky, Translated by Fan Ji

Three

In [Cultural Dawn], women's labor experience is far more complex than men's. Women are not only equal collaborators with men in society, but also surpass them in wisdom. Therefore, in a certain period of history, power in families, nations, and even tribes belonged to women. Ancient Greek writers said that among the Scythian and Slavic peoples, there was a type of female commune that owned land and other property. Undoubtedly, this situation also existed in the matriarchal clan system preserved by [Barbarians] (this matriarchal clan system still existed in the nineteenth century), such as the nobles of Verkhoyansk during the Tsarist era. From ancient Russian stories, one can also see the existence of such female communes among the Slavs. This ancient story says that a man from Ilya met his son, but the son did not recognize his father. Later, the mother pointed out a mark, and the son recognized him. The legend of the Amazons also says: The story of the ancient Serbian female hero [Alexander] mentions that there were female knight teams in the army of Alexander the Great. An old Czech legend also says that in the eighth century, women killed their husbands and defended themselves on high mountains, fighting successive wars with men for seven years. In Russian legends, there are also many stories of female heroes. Regarding women's intelligence and their conquest of the power of nature, such as the story of [Saint Vasilisa], they exist in the folk songs of various nations. [Female prophets], so-called shamans, female immortals, etc., can all be classified into this category. All of this suggests that, in addition to the natural wonder and special abilities of women, men in a certain period were dominated by women. Perhaps some [rules] were set up by women for self-defense and other reasons, to prevent men's necessary infringement during the last months of pregnancy, and to restrict the freedom of [strong men]'s actions.

Stories and legends have been preserved in large numbers. From Adam and Eve in the Bible, all unanimously say that women work for the devil, [not out of fear, but out of conscience]. They have no purpose of profiting themselves, but strive to do evil to mankind. Faust made a deal with the devil to regain his youth, but the witch did not try to regain her youth and beauty. Therefore, researchers of witches and witchcraft do not pay attention to this inexplicable fairness, although it is commonly believed that women's desire to remain young, healthy, and beautiful forever is also their flaw.

The struggle of men against the dominance of women in housework and life occurred simultaneously with the beginning of the disintegration of clans, the opposition between clans and families, and the development of private property. Men were influenced by women's rule for thousands of years. Later, he gradually broke away from being a laborer and became a worker, first as an assistant to women, then as an equal worker with women, and finally as the main labor force in cultivating land and making materials, especially in the period when they began to use their domesticated animals to transport things and plow the land. Men's position in the clan, unable to marry within his wife's clan or be an equal member of society, was not commensurate with the role he played in the economy. Therefore, in the following thousands of years, men waged a stubborn struggle, advocating that men be the heads of the family: advocating that children be recognized as men's children, not the children of their birth mothers, that children should belong to the father's clan, not the mother's clan: and advocating that private property be recognized as the private property of men and their clan, not the property of the wife and her clan. This struggle was very serious, because with the development of labor, women did not lag behind men, and she gradually became more skilled, experienced, and capable in her work. Men only had strength. Their struggle was a struggle to seize power, with the aim of depriving women of their life experience, and they finally achieved this goal 丨丨 conquering women and making [women men's domestic dogs].

Men even made the hearth the hearth of their clan. The myth of Prometheus stealing fire from heaven was probably fabricated by priests in the beginning. It deprived women of the merit of inventing fire, but later this myth became contrary to divine will.

Nothing comes from nothing. Although the stories of fighting female knights cannot be in the form as described in ancient legends, it is clear that they always existed in some way. [The Rape of the Sabine Women] (a story in ancient Italian history) can be said to be due to the lack of women in Rome. Not only was it necessary to plunder women because they were women, but also because women could spin yarn and weave cloth. [Kidnapping] girls can generally be explained as an attempt to steal good women from neighboring families to serve as slaves. (To be continued)

Women's Small Dictionary

— Wu

Women's Movement

[Women's Movement] is the struggle of women to break free from the shackles imposed on them by society for thousands of years and to seek freedom and equality for mankind. According to the current international situation, there are approximately two different tendencies: One is to demand that under the current social system, women can enjoy economic, political, and social equality with men 丨丨 In other words, women in this tendency only hope to improve the current situation and can consider themselves satisfied: The other is to believe that women's true liberation can only be realized by fundamentally transforming the society. Therefore, the means used by women belonging to this tendency are often more drastic than the former, and they are firmly united with men in the same tendency.

Women's Suffrage

[Women's Suffrage] refers to the fact that women have explicit provisions in the law to enjoy the same voting and eligibility rights as men in the landlord parliament and national assembly. The most prominent country in the world that grants women's suffrage is Wyoming in the United States (USA), followed by countries that have successively opened up the female ban. Differences in Suicide Methods Between Men and Women

— Translated from English

丨丨Statistics from British Scholars丨丨

Men and women have considerable differences in personality and emotions, which we can see in daily life. Dr. George Kirk, a British scholar, published the methods used by male and female suicides in Europe over the past twenty years, with the following differences:

Method　　Man　　　　　Woman

Hanging　　417　　240

Drowning　　152　　260

Self-mutilation　　207　　129

Poisoning　　79　　145

Shooting　　67　　2

Jumping down (from a high place)　　21　　36

Being run over　　24　　8

Other　　33　　18

The above figures are per 1,000 people.

According to the above, hanging is the most common for men, and drowning is the most common for women: Shooting and suicide on railways are more common among men, while poisoning and jumping down are more common among women. Hanging, self-mutilation, and suicide with a pistol, etc., require considerable preparation and are accompanied by terrifying feelings, which are generally not very chosen by women. Conversely, simple and easy methods such as poisoning and drowning seem to be more easily adopted by women.

Finance: Swap Prices Not Significant; Bid Price Retreats by More Than Three Yuan; August Futures Contracts Total 16,982; New September Contracts Total 25,830

The gold market was weaker yesterday, mainly because the bulls were arrogant before the swap, and the general shorts were apprehensive. Unexpectedly, the swap opened yesterday morning, with only the buying side posting a little over five yuan, which was only so-so. The Tianjin gang frantically sold spot goods, and the general bulls and spot firms bravely sold off futures bid prices. The selling pressure suddenly turned turbulent, and the last Guang gang and others purchased to stabilize the price after it broke through the 90-yuan mark. In the early morning, the overseas silver market in both the UK and the US showed a contraction, and the forward silver price on the five-gold exchange also fell by nine haos to four lis, but it was not as good as the opening. The exchange rate was extremely flat. London bullion rose one penny, US cotton rose 29 pound tones, and US wheat rose another 2.875 to 3.375. Stock prices had both ups and downs, and it seemed inappropriate to open high. However, due to the swap relationship, the over-the-counter pre-market trading opened relatively stable, but the key to the rise and fall at this moment depends on the level of the premium. Unexpectedly, the swap pre-market was quoted with the buying side posting five to six yuan. The general bulls liquidated, and even spot firms intended to sell off, resulting in a selling wind after the opening. Many major

bulls divested, and the sellers took the opportunity to be active. Spot firms also dumped. The HSBC listed exchange rates for both the UK and the US did not change, and the domestic market stepped down. The gold market then broke through the 90-yuan mark. Afterwards, swap rates were cheap and then expensive. The Guang gang and others took the opportunity to purchase contracts at low prices, and the exchange rate also slightly improved. There were still many buyers taking advantage of the low prices, and the situation turned stable. The price gradually rose but was still struggling. Afterwards, the swap rate stabilized, and the gold market also showed a stable state. The Seattle night market silver price reported a contraction of 25.125 and a half-point, and market sentiment was healthy. At noon, there was a lot of hesitation. The market situation fluctuated with the swap, which was very mediocre. The swap rate was quoted with the buying side posting four yuan to five yuan and seven jiaos. Flour and Wheat Skyrocket - Creates Opportunities for Foreign Flour and Wheat

The flour market, after opening this morning, showed signs of skyrocketing prices for each month. Sixth-grade wheat quotations, Chicago up another 90 jiao to 1 yuan 1 jiao, Canada up 34 jiao, coupled with persistent drought, hot and clear weather, and no signs of rain, rice prices rose sharply daily, causing widespread anxiety. Therefore, prices rose immediately after opening by 23%, after which various factories, due to the gradual increase in the prices of wheat, both in this port and outside the port, following the price of rice, and the difficulty of purchasing goods in the future, had no choice but to wait and see, unable to sell. Therefore, the sentiment outside the industry became firmer, gradually buying, and market prices gradually increased. Although real sales groups unanimously rejected it, and the Tianjin group remained motionless, the intensity of the sentiment did not diminish. This situation of continuous rise and increase is little different from the great flood of 1919. It is feared that the result of high prices will still require foreign wheat to be used for relief. As a result, this month rose 3%, AugustSeptember rose 4%7.5, October rose 5%2.5, November rose 5%, December rose 5.5%.

The wheat market showed an enthusiastic rise in prices for all months, with foreign wheat quotations up by a significant 349 jiao to 1 yuan 1 jiao. In addition, wheat prices in Suzhou, Wuxi, and other places also gradually followed the rise in rice prices, and in some places, they even exceeded the standard of Shanghai. As a result, market sentiment was stirred, and prices for each month jumped sharply after opening, rising by 56% to 10% compared to the previous day. By the opening of the afternoon session, due to the soaring flour market in the morning, market sentiment became even more turbulent. This month rose to 2 jiao 2 fen, August rose to 3 jiao 5 fen, September rose to 5 jiao 1 fen, October rose to 5 jiao 7 fen, November rose to 6 jiao 2 fen, December rose to 6 jiao 6 fen. Later, the leading bull traders released their positions, and prices saw a significant drop. Prices for September fell by 9% from the opening to the closing prices, while the rest fell by 35%, indicating that the market was not following normal rules amidst speculative frenzy. As a result, July still skyrocketed by 1 jiao 5 fen, August rose by 1 jiao 3 fen, September rose by 1 jiao 1 fen, October rose by 1 jiao 2 fen, November rose by 1 jiao 1 fen, and December rose by 9 fen. The spot wheat market also saw prices rise by 78% to 10% due to rice prices and standard relationships. The opening prices for Xuzhou wheat were 3 yuan 2 jiao 5 fen, Bengbu wheat 3 yuan 2 jiao 2 fen, Suzhou wheat 3 yuan 2 jiao 3 fen, Mingguang wheat 3 yuan 2 jiao, Baoying wheat 3 yuan 1 jiao 7 fen, Liuhe wheat 3 yuan 1 jiao 6 fen, Wuhu wheat 3 yuan, and Xinghua wheat 3 yuan 0 fen, with Fuxin and Fufeng each purchasing 5,000 bags.

Rice Prices Rise Daily

(South Shanghai) Yesterday, the supply from various groups for the 20th number (approximately 3,000 shi) was limited due to the extreme drought conditions, and prices rose steadily. Therefore, although the distribution routes were limited, prices soared easily. Today, the supply of rice from the packaging stomach has stopped, with only the local street taking action, and the tight situation is even more severe. The prices of the Changbang Su, Tong, and Nangang japonica rice have increased by another 56 jiao, while the prices of Qingjiao, Song, Si, and Xilian late rice have also risen by more than half a yuan. The prices of Duyangjian and Yinbianyuan and other varieties have also risen by more than 23 jiao.

(North Shanghai) Yesterday, the supply from various routes downstream was scarce due to drought and siltation of waterways, resulting in only ten or so ships arriving. The city's various types of distribution routes, white japonica and thin rice, continued to move, and the prices of white japonica and thin early rice rose again by 45 jiao. The supply of Baiyuan, Yangdu, and Jianling rice was still acceptable, and the prices also increased by 34 jiao. Customers from other ports, local streets, and surrounding rural areas made some transactions, and the prices increased by 2 jiao.

(Additional News) The current price increase is mostly due to market sentiment. The so-called "the more the price rises, the more people want to buy, and the more the price rises, the less people are willing to sell." Yesterday, it was heard that the central government was considering buying 500,000 shi of foreign rice to regulate the market if rice prices rise. This kind of rumor remains to be seen, but at the current rice prices, combined with the old sea dou, the number is not small. Looking back from the beginning to the most recent month ago, rice prices were very small. In less than a month, prices have risen by 45 yuan due to this year's drought, and the profit from hoarding rice is too high, causing great hardship to the general public.

Old Small Jiao Soars to Nine Yuan

Foreign Rice Will Take the Opportunity to Import

Foreign Rice Surges by 35 Jiao

Yesterday, the foreign rice market experienced skyrocketing prices, soaring again and again, with upward sentiment and extreme market tension. This was due to the recent hot and rainless weather, with reports of drought in various places, dried-up waterways, disrupted supply, and gradually decreasing arrivals. In addition, the rice-producing areas in the mainland were insufficient to meet their own needs and rushed to purchase rice from the Shanghai market. In recent days, in addition to the local hoarders who eagerly purchased rice, various groups from Yongshao, Chongsha, etc., also inquired about prices, making the cargo owners' sentiment even better. Hoarders only received and did not release rice, so the market repeatedly experienced price increases. Yesterday, 20,000 bags of small rice were offered, and 12,700 bags of various types of milled rice were offered. Machine-milled oil rice suddenly rose by half a yuan, with the highest price being 9 yuan 7 jiao, machine Jing rice rising to 9 yuan 3 jiao 5 fen, and oil milled rice rising to 8 yuan. Various milled rice from Hankou, Mingguang, and Shashi reached 7 yuan 56 jiao. The opening price of small rice was 8 yuan 8 jiao, and then it rose to 9 yuan. This rice, which was actually old rice from 1923, was able to fetch such a high price, and other rice prices were bound to rise one by one, which was 5 jiao and 34 jiao higher than the previous market. The sentiment of the hoarders remained strong, and they were still bullish on the market. However, by the afternoon, foreign firms such as Dafu and Yuanli had arrived on the market to solicit orders, because the local market price of Western small rice in Annam and Burma was already lower than the Shanghai market. Even with the addition of taxes, it could barely be profitable, but there was no high profit. Therefore, in addition to the above-mentioned two foreign firms, there were other foreign firms seeking to solicit orders. On the one hand, they planned to find ways to request tax reductions, so as to lower costs and indirectly allow poor people to obtain lower-priced rice. After this news spread throughout the market, old small rice fell by 12 jiao, and other rice prices stabilized. The last opening price of small rice was only 8 yuan 8 jiao 5 fen.
